Compilation Committee of Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Words

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Heaven Begins with Me (1)
<Prayer> This morning, may our Father look down upon us. On this third Sabbath morning of the month, we have come before the presence of our Father, pledging our sincerity. Just as You are holy, may You also make us holy, and just as You take responsibility for goodness, may You allow us to be those who take responsibility for goodness as well.
Our Father, who has overcome with infinite patience for the nation of Your desires, and who has come this far without concern for struggle, may we also be permitted to follow the cause of Your children. Knowing that You do not tolerate evil and that You are tirelessly expanding the stage for the practice of goodness, may we also be allowed to strive without rest.
Now, we, who bear the name of so-and-so, have bowed down before You. When was the moment we met and rejoiced in You, who delighted in our meeting according to goodness? What was the content that could not be omitted because we are Your beloved sons and daughters who love Your will? When was the time we resolved to unite with You and declared a common slogan to overcome the boundary of death? We must reflect on this once again.
Before our Father, we must fulfill our filial duty and take on the responsibility of sons. July 18, 1971 (Sunday) early morning, at the headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* This message is also included in <Words> No. 127 (published on August 28, 1971).
8   Heaven Begins with Me (1)
To pave the way that can bring joy to our Father, we must overcome the path of sorrow, and we know that the foundation of the desires our Father wishes cannot be achieved without overcoming the obstacles that stand before us. The place where sons and daughters who pledge to return glory and fulfill their filial duty should stand is a place where one swears to dedicate oneself entirely to our Father after overcoming the path of suffering. 
When we think of this, we long for the image of sons and daughters who want to proudly present themselves before all of heaven, claiming they have the qualifications to receive Your love while singing praises to You. You have also repeated the path of overcoming, and we are following that path.
When we think of this, if You shout, "This is it," we must also shout in response and pledge to advance until the final point where we can offer thanks and praise before You. Until now, even amidst difficult circumstances, we have put forth all our sincerity, but because it has not been enough, we must become sons and daughters who can fulfill our responsibilities before You with the hope that a new morning will come where our sincerity can reach.
As we reflect on whether we have become children who can be led to the point of unity that our Father desires and march according to Your command, Father, every time we discover You, who must always work hard to lead us, we cannot help but feel a humble heart.
When we think of the fact that our Father, who has worked so hard, must leave behind the labor of a thousand years because of us, we realize that the relationship between You and us, who should be praising the value of love, has become a relationship of shame and disgrace rather than one of joy. May each of us be able to look up to You as the one who is pitiful and the protagonist of love who cannot forget His sons.
When we consider that the standard of Your holy will is a path that must encompass nations and the world beyond the individual, we realize how difficult it is for us to move even our small selves and establish a standard of unity. We must reflect on how difficult a position our Father is in, who must lead the world. Now, we must become those who swear to not add to the difficulties before our Father.
Before placing our wishes before You and bowing our heads in prayer, we must become filial sons and daughters who worry about Your will. We must become loyal patriots and virtuous women for the future of our nation. Those who worry about the future of the nation, who spend sleepless nights with anxiety as their friend, do not sing songs along with their life’s desires, but rather have become a group that knows the path of suffering that lies ahead and advances with sighs.
History is inherited through such groups, and when we think of how the baton is passed to these groups, running toward the hopes of tomorrow and the foundation of happiness beyond, we must recognize that when we fail to advance toward our goals with a sense of urgency, those who run on behalf of heaven will succumb to those who run on behalf of Satan.
Satan exists based on the material world, while heaven is based on the intangible realm. Therefore, we must understand how fearful and terrifying this realm of the flesh is for humans living within the realm of life that cannot escape the tangible influence of Satan.
When we consider that the flesh can capture the heart and prevent a person from stepping out from the position You desire, we must stand before our Father with strong bodies. This strength must be strong for the sake of goodness but also strong against evil. Our hearts must not be weak in the places where we desire. We must be strong. What must we be strong for? We must be strong for goodness. We must also be strong against evil. Our Father has spoken of weak hearts before goodness and strong bodies before evil, but we must be strong in both aspects.
What the heart desires is not the wish of one individual but the wish of the whole that history desires. To fulfill this wish, our hearts and bodies must be strong, so we must indeed resemble our Father. We must become sons and daughters who can represent our Father’s usual appearance, and we earnestly hope and wish to become such sons and daughters.
Father, now that we have passed the halfway point of 1971 and are welcoming the third Sabbath morning, may You grant us love and compassion. Now, when there are sons and daughters who wish to come and share their inner feelings with You, may this be a place where we can meet our Father, who comes freely and naturally, rather than with anxious eyes before the environment of the enemy.
Each of our hearts and bodies must be captured by You, and while we always come before You, You carry us, but we have been playing the opposite role. We try to follow Your movements, but we have always been in the opposite position. When we see this, we realize that we cannot move beyond our current position without stepping on the victorious foundation of desires that can win and advance.
Until now, our Father, who has come forth through countless ancestors throughout history, is still our Father who cannot help but do so on our behalf in this era. We must understand the heart of our Father, who cannot retreat or turn back.
Now, may we hold onto Your hand, embrace Your neck, follow for what You desire, wipe away Your tears, and become sons and daughters who can remove those traces of tears, saying, "Do not walk the path of labor for me, but go for the nation and the world."
Our faith life has become habitual. It has been so in the past, it is so in the present, and it will be so in the future. When we think about this, how can such a group in this position urge the factors of happiness before our Father and become the sons and daughters of tomorrow’s parents? In the past, we drove our Father into a painfully long path of suffering, and seeing that even today, we are a group that shakes our heads in refusal despite receiving our Father’s requests, we gather here as those who have never left the position of unfilial children. Father, please come again.
We know that a true stimulus and a new shock are needed, so please come with Your love, Your hopes, and Your circumstances. May You meet sons and daughters who can be in harmony with Your hopes and circumstances, and may You be the Father who can discuss victories for the future from the position of victory in history.
This morning, may You look down upon Your many sons and daughters scattered across the nation. As we are moving into the hot summer days, please remember Your daughters who are on the front lines. Since You are raising them and going with them, may they come to know that the front lines they are on are the heavenly front lines, and the places they are fighting are the heavenly strongholds.
When we think that those who do not know this and flee from that position can only be considered as traitors before You, we must understand that the standard of good and evil is also present in today’s Unification Church. While there are good daughters, there are also those who bring sorrow to You, and when we realize that there are groups that should not exist, Father, please do not let Your shameful appearance be revealed through those who remain on the front lines.
When we think that You are the protagonist with the ability to move the world centered around one person, may You take our one life as a foundation for indemnity and establish a foundation of victory for the whole, while also preparing a foundation that can be praised before the nation and the world. Father, we earnestly hope that we may become those who remain true.
Just because there are those who want to go does not mean they should be the standard, and we should not set the standard for those who cannot hold their position. We must become a group that advances toward the enemy with new resolutions, worthy of being honored before heaven and loved by the people of heaven, and we earnestly hope that we may become praised children.
May You raise Your children scattered across the nation, and if they cannot become the embodiment of Your wishes and cannot help before Your will, please take action to settle this during this period. Thus, may You expand a pure and clean foundation without shame in laying the groundwork for a new historical tradition, so that all nations and peoples can praise You without lacking anything.
This morning, may You be personally present wherever the Unification groups gather. As Your sons and daughters scattered across the world pledge their sincerity toward this one side of Korea in Asia, may Your blessing be connected to that place through the lifeline, and may there be Unification workers fighting in foreign lands, considering the foreign people as their own lives and thinking of the path of sacrifice as their own path of sin. When we think of this, we must not become a shameful sight gathered here. Father, protect us, allow us to go, and grant us the permission to advance.
Just as You bless them, may those who should receive blessings through similar actions be the children who remain here. May we firmly realize that we must not become a nation that can perish, saying, "I will remain comfortable while others toil," while pledging loyalty to heaven.
May we be allowed to be heavenly sons and daughters who pledge to advance toward the day of hope for tomorrow. We know that there are Your children who are eagerly awaiting meetings and discussing new news day and night with heaven. Father, who is the Lord of all blessings, may You be the center of their lives and their wishes, and may we become glorious sons and daughters who are not ashamed before the world, as heaven praises that it has found such sons and daughters until the day we can meet You.
We believe that the children who bow down here, regardless of age, are not a problem. Even if they are very old, if their longing for You is more intense than that of the young, heaven knows that it is with that person. Even if they are young boys and girls, if there are those who say they will walk this path despite the intertwining of life, please allow them to fulfill the hopes of Your sons and daughters and make them the heroes of the founding of the heavenly nation.
We entrust this day to You, and we earnestly wish that wherever tears are shed in Your holy name, the foundation of Your glory will be expanded and the bonds of life will deepen.
Please take charge of this one hour. May You manifest Yourself and lead our hearts and bodies to pave the way for victory so that we can offer thanks before You. We earnestly ask this, and we pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.
<Words> When we look at this world we live in, this world is...
We know that the desired heavenly kingdom is not yet realized. Because of this, we understand that this world is a place devoid of good people, a place where we cannot place our hopes as true humans.  
We live on this earth, but we know that our living is not out of desire but rather out of necessity. When we ask whether there is anyone who can proudly declare to the world or to the ages that they possess the happiness they have longed for in their hearts, we find that there is no such person. No matter how much one may be revered by many, when asked about their own happiness, they can only say that they are more unhappy than anyone else. This is the condition of humanity.  
Such humanity has woven the world until now, and we know that the world cannot rejoice with such humanity. It is a world that groans, faced with the fate of having to judge the crossroads of tomorrow's hope.  
Religious people seeking heaven in a wicked reality  
Among such a world, we recognize that certain groups are seeking heaven and pursuing a new country. These groups are not ordinary people living in society. They are not necessarily educated individuals or artists. They are not those who stand in positions that can be recognized by the public, but rather those who live quietly, yearning for heaven and living righteously without public acknowledgment. We know that these groups are religious people.  
Among religions, there are those responsible for the east, those for the south, or perhaps for the west and the center... Although they have different responsibilities, there are groups that live their lives with great effort, hoping for uncertain goals, trying to regulate their present lives and adjust their hopes for tomorrow. We know that these groups are religious people. Therefore, religious people are not those who live centered on themselves but rather those who must align their lives with the direction dictated by the ideals of religion.  
Within religions, there are various sects, and among religious people, there are individuals with different circumstances. Because people's circumstances differ, the directions they follow will also differ, and we understand that the hopes people have in their real lives will vary accordingly.  
Take a person named A. If A's life journey is solely oriented towards the east, they may be happy, but if they must go west with their physical body while heading east, they cannot progress towards the east nor can they go west. Here, we find ourselves at a crossroads, faced with the question of whether to become someone who only goes east or someone who only goes west, and we know that we must overcome this moment of anguish.  
Human beings in the position of choosing the path of goodness  
No matter how excellent a religion one believes in, we must ask whether one is in a position to devote their body and mind entirely to the religion they believe in. The path to that position requires overcoming a path of suffering. The standard for overcoming this is not simply to overcome the limits of the heaven one desires. If there is a heaven worth ten, one must overcome an environment of ten difficulties. This cannot be the case. If one desires a heaven worth ten, one must have the resolve and determination of a hundred or a thousand to leave behind the foundation of that heaven. This is the path of our lives that you all know well.  
When we ask whether we can find an environment that cooperates with the purpose of starting anew with the will of heaven, we find that we cannot meet such an environment. Among those living in such an environment, are there people who center their cooperation around their own desires? Rather than cooperating, there are those who take advantage of me, undermine me, block my path, and even sacrifice me to harm and oppose me.  
However, if there are those who recognize that this path is a fateful road they cannot avoid and resolve to walk it, their resolve must not be merely to seek a heaven worth ten but rather to pledge for a heaven worth a hundred, a thousand, or ten thousand. Without such a resolve, one will exhaust their commitment through the torment of surrounding circumstances. Only by possessing a content greater than ten can one enter heaven; if one is equipped with a standard less than ten, they will inevitably collapse at the gates of heaven. When we consider this, we understand how arduous our lives are as we strive to commit to goodness and choose the path of goodness.  
No one is unaware in their heart. Everyone knows, without needing to be told, that "that person is a good person." After spending a day, a month, or a year, everyone knows who the good people are in their community. There is no one who lacks the ability to discern good from bad. Everyone knows and can distinguish, but it is hard to find someone willing to step forward and take that position.  
Today, if we look at a village with a hundred houses, everyone knows who the good person is among them, but how many people are willing to voluntarily step forward and say, "I will surely go that way"? They know, they can discern, and they can speak, but how many are willing to take the lead and say, "I will definitely go"? Finding a starting point to begin anew is more challenging than any warrior or hero heading into battle.  
If there is a struggle, it is a game that determines victory or defeat based on a moment, but the path of goodness cannot be determined by a single moment. The determination and judgment of goodness is not based on a moment, a year, or even ten years; it is a path that must be walked throughout one’s life. Therefore, while everyone knows what is good, why is it that they cannot take responsibility and say, "I will go"?  
The place where goodness resides cannot be confined to a moment. Goodness accompanies eternity; it does not merely accompany the history of the present but also the history of the future, and it must relate to the whole. When we consider that goodness is intertwined with eternity, the future, and the whole, it must be a content that can go to the eternal end and return. To relate to the whole, one must surpass the whole.  
When we look at this issue, we can discover where goodness resides, but to relate to that place, we must risk our lives to go there. This is an undeniable fact.  
The path of goodness  
No matter how well one has done for ten years, a single day of failure can ruin those ten years on the path of goodness. Even if one has worked hard for ten years, a single moment of error can render all that effort futile. If someone has spent half their life striving towards the stage of goodness without leaving any blemish, yet makes a mistake at the border of half their life, the merits they have built up will not be presented as complete goodness before God or as something to be shown to history; instead, it will conclude as incomplete goodness.  
From this perspective, the path towards goodness must conclude with one’s entire life. We humans understand this, but we cannot proceed because we know that the path of goodness requires continuous advancement throughout our lives. Everyone knows the good path, can judge good people, and knows how to become good, but they cannot proceed because it is difficult for those living in this present world.  
So why must goodness be this way? Because goodness is eternal. The more one walks the path of goodness, the more joy increases rather than sorrow. As one progresses, they do not descend but ascend towards higher places, and the higher they rise, the broader their perspective becomes, allowing new global connections to form, which brings joy. In walking the path of goodness throughout one’s life, one must aim their perspective towards higher places; otherwise, they cannot reach the highest standard of goodness that life desires.  
Today, countless people hope for heaven. They long for an ideal world. They yearn for a more peaceful world. Above all, where does that world of peace begin? Does it start from the end that anyone can reach, or does it begin from a higher place? If one ends their efforts and sincerity at the place they have reached in this fallen human world, that place may be the endpoint of the fallen world, but it cannot be the destination of the ideal world created by God. While it may serve as the endpoint of the fallen world, it cannot be the endpoint of heaven.  
Then what is the standard for living one’s life? Is heaven a place where God is present and all creation can praise happiness? It is not. The place where one has brought all their sincere efforts is not a place where we can eternally dwell centered around heaven; it can only serve as a starting point for a new beginning.  
Heaven is like a high mountain. Some people start here (①) and only go up a little before coming back down. The center is here (②). Others may go a little higher before coming back down. The higher one climbs, the closer they get to the center. Based on this highest peak (⑧), humanity progresses. Some people may reach here (⑦) in their lifetime and then retreat. Of course, those who start and then immediately retreat need not be considered, but those who reach here (⑦)—just a little more to the peak—before falling also fall in the same way. If one falls from here (⑦), the suffering is proportionally greater. When one person suffers, it does not end with that one person; many who followed them will also suffer because of that one person.  
From this perspective, the higher one climbs, the greater the damage when they fall. Therefore, while God desires to allow the path centered around global religions in every way, He stands in a position where He cannot allow it. Why? To prevent causing too much harm. Thus, the true path of goodness remains a path that has yet to be sought. If someone climbs to this standard (⑦) and then falls, the damage can completely block the history of future generations.  
The path to the summit  
When we consider religion, those who pursued and followed it can reach the highest peak, but if they fall at the nine-tenths mark, they may have been close to reaching the summit of the whole, yet if they fail to advance even a step and fall, the damage does not end with them; it influences the entire religious community and can completely block the door of that religion for distant descendants. You must understand that many such facts have occurred throughout the historical process among those who have sought the providential will.  
When we think about this, there are hurdles to overcome in order to break through to the summit of religion. How does one ascend to the summit? Since it is not a path that one has pioneered based on their own foundation of religion, to find the way up to the summit, one must either unite completely with the leader or go alone. There are only these two paths. While one might think, "I can just go up," that is not possible. That would be abnormal. It cannot happen. There are only two paths: either one climbs themselves or holds onto someone else to go up.  
If one reaches the summit, they will inevitably encounter a new dimension of the world. (Pointing to <Figure 1>) This (A) represents the inner world, and this (B) represents the outer world. It means one can see a world that corresponds to a new dimension. If one falls from here (⑧), this side (A) becomes empty. There is no area created here. The area cannot exist. This side (A) is void, empty.  
Therefore, even if one has gone through all the paths of suffering and reached the highest peak, when we consider the ultimate issue, one must still go beyond it. One should not only desire to climb to the top but must have the resolve to go beyond the peak. One must be strong enough to have the capacity to go beyond the peak to continue on the path.  
Those who think that simply reaching the summit is sufficient will not succeed. Isn’t that so? The summit is a place where one can see both the aspect of ascending and the aspect of descending. While descending may be easy, ascending is difficult. Here, there is another issue. Here, one must make a new start. If one does not take the initiative in their starting point, they will only have the path of following. There are only two paths.  
Here (below the summit), there are two paths to ascend, but here (at the summit), there are also two paths to ascend. Even if one climbs towards a new summit, that cannot become the eternal foundation of heaven. It cannot serve as a foundation where the whole world can rest. Nor can it be a foundation for the establishment of the heavenly kingdom; because one has not settled their relationship with the world, they cannot be in a position where the world and heaven can connect. This must be settled.  
At the summit, there is divergence. This direction (①) and that direction (②)...
This will intersect. The lower part rises up, and the upper part comes down. The left becomes the right, and the right becomes the left. In this intersecting form, we must see a new beginning. The origin of heaven starts here (③). (Refer to <Figure 2>)

That is why the Bible says, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." Heaven is not at the end of the world I desire, but within my heart. What kind of place is that heart? It is not a place that is one with all the factors of this world where death surges, but a base where a wave of the gift of life can spread by overcoming it. We must not stop from there (the summit) but seek the new values of life from there and become the people of heaven who bear the mission to build heaven. 

Heaven begins where the heart and body are united. It cannot be found in the world of the body. It does not exist in this world. Therefore, that starting point must be determined from within my heart, and it is a place where I can practice and realize what I envision in my heart, aligning with it. By finding that one place, we can welcome heaven.

That is why heaven does not come through any future end world, but it comes by drawing a starting point from one’s own heart and coming along with that starting point. When we weigh it around that starting point, it becomes a support point that can make the balance beam horizontal. It is like that support point. That support point must not only be horizontal. While the purpose of the balance is to be horizontal, it must tilt to the right. It must not tilt to the left. It must tilt to the right. That tilting to the right is the beginning. It is the ability to turn back and go to the right anew...

While the horizontal can serve as a purpose to determine a new point, it cannot serve as a starting point to shift to a new direction. It may be a point, but it cannot encompass the entire content that can shift the direction. That is the beginning. It is the starting point for shifting the direction. This is an undeniable fact.

Similarly, where does heaven come from? It starts from the heart. Where in the heart? It starts from a heart that has overcome the world. This is how it is. No matter how much heaven may touch me environmentally, if my heart is evil, if my heart cannot envision it, and if my heart cannot resonate with it, then even if heaven comes, that heaven is useless. Therefore, the foundation that can welcome heaven is not the environment but myself. I am the problem. The support point that can maintain heaven is my heart, preceding the environment.

In that sense, where is heaven? The disciples who were following could not resolve reality, and they saw the future heaven as a foundation of happiness, with a sense of global authority and success. Jesus broke that fundamental idea and said, "The kingdom of heaven is within you." A person who cannot envision the heaven of the heart cannot move that heaven even if it becomes an environmental heaven. Without a firm decision in the heart, one cannot take complete action. Complete action arises from complete determination.

That is why how much does your heart yearn for goodness? That yearning must unite with historical goodness. No matter how painful the environment may be, one must overcome it to walk alongside goodness. No matter how lonely the historical end environment may be, one must not evade it but break through it. Such a heart must pave the way for unchanging work, and from that determination, the living environment of the body that can become one with that heart must be resolved and determined, for heaven begins there. Heaven is not found where the heart and body act separately. The advance toward the direction of heaven begins from where the heart and body are united; heaven does not occur where the actions of the heart and body are divided.

From that perspective, what Jesus preached is that we must not tilt left or right centered around the content that can unite the heart and body. Rather, we must eliminate the environment and possess the subjectivity that can prepare for the weighted steps of advancement to welcome heaven.

Heaven does not come from others, nor by others. It comes from me. Because we are fallen humans, we must deny ourselves. If I cannot go myself, and if I cannot present this, then someone else will present it. When someone else presents it, I must become one with them to go to heaven. I must follow them. I must absolutely align with them. If they go east, I must go east too. If they go east and I say I will go west, or if I have the heart that says I shouldn’t do what they did, I must not have that mindset. There must be no criticism there.

There are only two paths. If I am to take the path I must follow, but I cannot become the one who can carry out that principle, what should I do? I must not say, "This is my path, so I will do it my way." At that time, I must go through someone else. Who is that someone else? It is someone who can serve as a standard before humanity. That is why many religions have emerged to teach that someone to humanity.

Because fallen humans cannot go by themselves, they must follow. There is no other way but to follow. Following does not mean coming in search of a center. (Refer to <Figure 3>) Wouldn’t it be wonderful if that were possible? It is not possible to find a center and stop there. I am not looking for a specific place in the world to go towards. The center we must go to is not before humanity. Isn’t that so?

Where should the world go? Where is the center that has been the standard of happiness that humanity has longed for throughout history? Where is the center of the world? We are searching for it now. Is it in the communist world? Is it in the democratic world? No. Is it in the path our father is taking? No. Is it in the path our village leader is taking? No. Is it in the path our country’s leader is taking? No. Then is it the path of some leader who can represent Europe when centered on the world? No. Then when centered on the democratic world or the communist world, can we discover that center? No. That center cannot be found.

That center cannot be found alongside human history. It cannot be found connected to the stage of human life; it is somewhere else. The center that has emerged with a different purpose is religion. This is said in light of the fallen world. When one aims for a center and reaches the results of that purpose, humanity's history can urge happiness and establish the origin of peace in the world, but that is not found on the earth. In other words, such a base cannot be established through human brains, human organizations, or human systems. It cannot be determined through those means.

So where should we start? We must start from heaven. From whom should we start? Not from a well-believing leader, but from the master who guides the leader. Who is that master? It is God. We must start from God.

That is how it is. Therefore, as the end approaches, everything becomes ambiguous. It was said that the family is the center, but the family is becoming ambiguous. It was said that the nation is the center, but that is also becoming ambiguous. It was said that ideology is the center, but that too has become ambiguous. Now, what remains? Even love has become ambiguous.

Before humanity, family is precious, the nation is precious, and the world is precious. This was the foundation of hope. However, even though we thought parents were precious, and that the leader of the nation was precious, and that some leader who could represent the world was precious, it is not that.

Even the love that was proclaimed as absolute, to the point of exchanging one’s life, has now become ambiguous. Isn’t that so? Is there anyone who pursued love in a place where a man and a woman could sacrifice their lives for each other and praise eternal happiness? That is what is said, but even that love has become ambiguous. There is nothing that can present a true family, a true nation, a true world, or true love. That is the end times.

In the end times, everything becomes faint. Because it started from something faint, the end also becomes faint. In that faint place, one cannot recognize a definite self. That time is precisely now. Isn’t that so? Throughout history, all humanity has searched for a center, but that center point has become ambiguous. It cannot be found solely by humanity, nor can it be decided by gathering humanity together; it stands at a point of historical termination.

Therefore, where must the center point start? It must start from the heart. That heart is not the kind of heart that people in today’s world have, but a heart that can sacrifice one’s life for goodness and can sacrifice one’s entire self for goodness. It must start from a standard centered on goodness, where one can deny oneself countless times. It is not from a position that can affirm oneself; it is not centered on that heart of mine. In other words, if you have entered the 80% mark, you must become a standard of goodness that can be recognized as a starting point to overcome this border. The standard of goodness must be able to represent the whole in relation to eternity.

This must be the case because history must not govern goodness; rather, history must be governed by that goodness. Personality cannot govern goodness at will; rather, the standard of goodness creates personality. It is not that people create goodness; rather, goodness must create people. The world governed by heaven and heavenly principles

How do we know whether there is electricity or not? We can know by seeing the light that appears when electricity acts. When electricity flows, it must cause action.

How does that action occur? Action cannot occur independently. There is nothing in the world that acts independently. There is nothing in all matters of the world that operates independently. There is no independent action in all realms of action. That is how it is. Isn’t that so? When there is action, there is always give and take. The conditions of the environment already encompass this.

You see, right? When I say, "I am happy," do I just feel happy alone? I feel happy because there is an object of that happy action.

Action requires relative conditions. Everything in the material world or the world of natural phenomena is felt through the action phenomena of relative rights; if it does not go through action, it cannot be felt. Therefore, action cannot be done alone. There is no independent action. Relative conditions are absolutely necessary for action.

In this light, the saying "conscience acts alone" cannot exist. Without a subject and an object, action absolutely cannot occur. Whether or not it can be sorted out is not my responsibility. How much sincerity do you put in while spreading for God? That’s the question. I think of the problem like that. It’s not about whether it will be sorted out or not. You must put in more sincerity than the person responsible for sorting it out. Such sorting will not harm Heaven. If God does not push this, how will the will be fulfilled? 

These days, when I see our members, since they say they will get paid at the newspaper company, it seems like the dead spirits of those who have not received their salaries are clinging to them, and they all want to go there. Some people say, “Even if I go out into the world to work, I should have authority and position, so shouldn’t I be given a name based on the standards of success?” To such people, I want to give them a reality check. These kids! Did the Unification Church leader Moon Sun-myung teach you that?
before, should we drink kimchi soup before deciding whether to eat rice cake? Such people do not last long and must be cut off. It must be done for the whole. This is what I told the national tour leaders this year. I said we must establish ourselves centered on a subjective ideology. I urged them to remain faithful to the responsibilities of the church until the end. No matter what else there is, there is something they must accomplish. If I am a red bean in a barley field, I must bear fruit as a red bean in that barley field. One must have a firm belief that they will not move until God moves them.

Heaven begins with me (1)
Do you still want to shine like the sun while you are struggling in the mountains and fields? For whom? For that certain someone? That is unnecessary. It is just that you cannot do it now, but if you wait a little longer, you will turn things around. That is why a fresh start is necessary. Here comes Mr. Kim. Who do you like more, Mr. Kim or the Son of God? It is not about Mr. Kim. That Mr. Kim will break the jar. He does not think about going to the bottom and being a servant, does he? Here is Jang Young-chang as well... Those who want to be high must be brought low. Those who want to be low will be raised. That is the principle. That is the main thought of unification ideology.

But are you searching for a bowl of rice because of a rice bowl? The teacher has lived without worrying about living expenses for this month with his mother. If he has money, he would scrape it together to spend it elsewhere. But that does not mean he will starve to death. He has lived his whole life like that. 

Does the Unification Church's Teacher Moon not know the painful things that happen centered on his family? The teacher himself has often reached a point where he wanted to pick up an apple that fell in the restroom without regard for his dignity. Out of concern for his dignity and the prestige of the Son of God, he could not do that. From this perspective, today you all are the ones seeking heaven. Heaven is not achieved in the world of others. It starts from within yourselves.

Every time you look at yourselves in the mirror, you should think, "This nose looks greedy! These eyes are filled with the poison of a viper! These hands have the claws of an eagle! My heart is filled with the nails of a murderer and arrows! This child of mine! I must make him suffer and cut off his head." This is the kind of play you need to engage in. Eating comfortably, if you did not have lunch, you should find lunch, and if you did not have dinner, you should find dinner. When do you think you can do all that and go to heaven? Absolutely not. The teacher himself often misses lunch, forgets about sleep, and everything else while engaging in this play... The system is out of order. 

When we look at all this, what is the Unification Church's Teacher Moon fighting for? He is not fighting for a global heaven. As the one responsible for leading the Unification Church, I am fighting to not be burdened by my conscience, to not lose my personal heaven. That is the conclusion. 

If you live comfortably, you must repent. Ultimately, the heaven of the environment does not come automatically. Who is the source and motivation for that? Shouldn't it be me, as the leader? Yes, if you sleep well and wake up, you must repent. If you eat well and put down your spoon, you must repent. If you have met comfortable days, you must repent. If not, you will perish. With that heart of repentance, when you pray for the whole to be blessed and for the foundation of rest for all, even if that person tries to perish, God will not let it happen. Even if Satan tries to strike, he cannot. Isn't that so? 

In the world, if you have made a mistake, you must honestly say you were wrong for forgiveness and compassion to occur, right? There is room for sympathy, but if you act arrogantly after doing well, there will be nothing left. From this perspective, heaven begins in my heart.

Then, is the Unification Church's Teacher Moon not ashamed in front of his family? The other day, on Sunday, from morning to night, for thirteen hours, he spoke and went to Cheongpyeong. Even though it was pouring rain, the family members were digging the ground. They had no choice but to fulfill their responsibilities on the designated date. As soon as he arrived, he was so tired that he could not sit down and spread out a blanket to sleep, so he stretched his legs and leaned against the blanket inside the tent, opening his mouth and snoring. Then he woke up to the sound of snoring. When he looked outside, it was pouring rain, and the family members were digging the ground with pickaxes and pulling carts. Seeing that made him cry.

If God were to come here, what would happen? If God were to give the final notice during the course of Teacher Moon's life, what would he do? Because Teacher Moon has that heart, even if those people are tired, they want to look at him and do their best. 

These days, they say many warrants have come out? Many people say they will go because of the emergency drills, but how many are willing to come? When it ends, who will come? If no one comes, that person is not someone who works with a sincere heart. 

The other day, a young man from Yeosu received a telegram from his father after 23 years. While working, he received the telegram and said, "Satan has appeared." I thought, "If Satan has appeared, how will you act, and how will you deal with Satan?" At first, I did not give him a penny. I gave him 2,000 won and sent him to go and come back. "This guy, even though he said Satan has appeared, let’s see if there is any news." But this guy came back yesterday. "Hey, you! You have met the conditions. Before the standard I desire, before God, you have become someone who can boast about having built this building. You came well." 

Everyone is hoping to go because it is hard, but that person who returned is truly a Unification Church person. Such people, those who have gone and returned, can have more shining content among those who work than those who have not gone or those who have stayed and worked. Why? Because they have not yet been tested. You have not stood in the position of being commanded, you have not been able to go to the position of acting, and you have not been able to stand in the decisive position of being able to decide whether to do this or that, so whom should you trust? You should trust those who have gone and returned. That is why I am thinking about what to buy when I go today. So, should I not buy anything? If I only buy for that person, others will say, "Why only for that person?" (laughter) That should not happen. 

From this, we can see that the Unification Church's Teacher Moon has a truly difficult fate. Even if he sleeps and wakes up, he must pray while lying down. Shouldn't it be so? Even while sleeping, there are Unification Church members scattered around the world praying to receive blessings, right? Shouldn't it be so? In our country, it is night, but in America, it is day. Aren't they praying while sweating and shedding blood? When they pray for the teacher in Korea, can God handle all of that for me? They must be tired and need to sleep now, right? Because that humble heart does not disappear from the Unification Church's Teacher Moon, the foreign members are in a frenzy wanting to see him. Do you understand? They must want to see him and want to meet him. 

If there is something that weighs on your conscience, you cannot welcome heaven. When you get your seal, you bury it deep in the iron box, right? Now, all the property worth over 1 billion is registered in the teacher's name, and if someone wanted to take it and cheat, they could do so easily. However, I do not carry my seal around in my back pocket. "If someone wants to take it, let them try. If I have dedicated myself based on justice, then use it." This is it. If you cannot do that and come out with your face and prestige, I do not like it. Such a person will never let this go. I would rather give it to someone who says they do not want it than to someone who insists on having it. That is the teacher's attitude toward life.

What will happen if you do that? When you ask who motivated you, if it is not for heaven, it will make that person a thief. By doing so, it gets blocked. You must understand that. You should not have that kind of mindset. 

The path to heaven centered on your heart is nothing else. It is for the nation, for the world, for humanity... That is endless. If it is difficult, it is difficult. Always the heart is tightening... 

When you quietly observe the world, you will see that those in public office are pitiful. They have given their utmost sincerity, but if they make a mistake before their intention, and if a thousand years of merit is ruined because of me, what will happen? It is like a debtor who has no money but the time to repay the debt is running out, that is the feeling. I have been living like that until now. 

Some people say that the Unification Church's Teacher Moon has now succeeded in the world. The other day, when I was talking to a university president, he said, "Teacher Moon has succeeded more than an ordinary person, hasn't he? From any perspective, the Unification Church has succeeded. Teacher Moon's name will remain in history, won't it?" What does it matter if the name remains in history? Even if he has gained the great honor of remaining in history, if he is far from the world of heart when he goes to that place, what will he do? How will he face that shame? 

What does it matter to succeed in the world? He will die... When he dies, he will go to that place centered on God. If he becomes a heart rebel in that place, what will he do? To say that he has succeeded... Success can rather be a disaster. This always tries to trip my left foot and my right hand, trying to push me aside from all directions. This is ultimately a snare. 

In the end, one must know that what they love the most can become their enemy and must handle it well without being burdened by their conscience. Without creating a path in front of their conscience, they cannot welcome heaven even if they go to heaven. You must remember that you yourself are the problem. 

<Prayer> You love the Unification Church. The more I think about that love, the more I realize that there must be a Father who is for the Unification Church. Do we love the Father? We have now realized that we must be for the Father. I thought heaven came from God, and I thought it came from some teacher, but now I have clearly realized that heaven begins with me. 

Who will find the nation I must find, and who will find the world I must find? Those who have not felt the sorrow of losing the world will not need the world. Those who have not felt the sorrow of losing the nation will not even think about seeking the nation. When a person who has had a nation, a tribe, and a family loses them, those who have not had them may not know, but those who have had them know how bitter it is. 

I must become a son of heaven who can represent the world, and I must represent the nation, the tribe, the family, and all people. When I think about this fact, that place is not a place where I am alone. When I go, the Father in heaven must follow me. When I stay in my family, the Father must come here. When I stay in the church, the Father must come to me. When I stay in my workplace, the Father must come to me. When I go for the nation, He must come to me. On the path toward the world, I must not go in a lonely position at any time, but I must live a life of devotion and sincerity that cannot escape from the heavenly heart and heavenly will. 

If there is something I long for, I must long for the world you want to find, and I must long for the nation you want to find. Also, we must love individuals who can represent the nation more than those who are in the nation, and we must love individuals who can represent the world more than those who are in the world. When we think about this fact, such a person must become one who carries the heart of the Father and one who has the love of the Father. 

I have realized that the Father is always advising me through my conscience. The conscience commands me to overcome the environment and to sacrifice in the environment, but I have regarded it as an enemy. 

Why is this in my heart to torment me? Paul lamented, "Oh, wretched man that I am," and we must overcome the position where two factors block each other and do not correspond. 

We must be grateful that we have not met the day of death as the reality of the vow we had already prepared for death. 

Whether in a place of hunger, in a place of nakedness, in a place of disgrace, in a place of pioneering, or even if my body is torn and cut, when I can forget myself and be in a place that only comforts the Father, I know that I will not perish. I thought you were not there in such a place, but you were there, and I thought you were far from me, but I did not recognize that you were very close. 

The heart inside our bodies beats continuously 24 hours, but because it is too close, there are many times we do not feel it, right? Not feeling that you are very close is similar to not knowing because you are in a very close and deep place. We were poor beings who thought you were far away, and we did not know that you were living with us, resting with us, and living with us. We must become those who can discover that you are with us. 

Now, when we ask where the world of love is and seek that path, we have realized that there are no remaining groups that come out with themselves. Only in the place of sacrifice, only in the place of serving the whole, can one remain. This is the principle of heaven's way and the principle of human nature. We must clearly understand that development comes from here. 

When we see someone who speaks with anger and criticizes others, thinking that they are like a prince of heaven or a princess of heaven, we must understand that they are extremely foolish. 

I have realized that if there are sons and daughters who want to become embodiments of meekness and humility, who want to become sacrificial offerings and dedicate themselves to the whole, who long for the nation and the world, and who endure all kinds of suffering to overcome their current position, they will absolutely not perish. I have known that when I walked that path, the Father was with me, and when I lay down in a lonely place, the Father was there with me, shedding tears and embracing me, staying up all night with me.
I stood in a place asking for forgiveness, realizing that it was not because of something new, but because I was far from my father. I understood that my father had already encouraged me and given me new hope.

Father, please take charge of the path that the Unification Church must follow in the future. No matter how excellent or admirable we may be on this earth, we know that we cannot reach the holiness of the Father, and we cannot meet relative factors in front of the Father's absolute standard. If there is something good, it must bear fruit for You, and if there is something to boast about, it must be presented before You. I have come to understand that the world that must leave behind this traditional thought is the world of the heart of unification, so please allow us to run that path beautifully.

When I think about the fact that there is still life left in the footsteps that were prepared for a doomed fate, I must be grateful. I did not know that in the place where I sought the Father with blessings and patience amidst resentment and curses, I would encounter an environment where I could honor the Father centered on the bond of heart.

I sincerely hope that today’s members of the Unification Church will recognize that they should feel ashamed of themselves and be grateful for the great price of the Father’s hard work. The path of faith must not be devoid of tears. Please help us to realize that we must not suppress the painful heart that seeks a foundation of comfort for a moment, forgetting food and clothing, and that we must take steps of overcoming.

When there is no one named Moon Amuga in the Unification family today, and when asked who can lead this Unification family in accordance with the Father’s will, if there are sons and daughters who can step forward and say it is I, please bestow abundant blessings upon them. Please promise a thousandfold and ten thousandfold the authority that the teacher possesses, which was promised through the teacher. The members of the Unification Church must be that vanguard. When the misfortune approaches this country, who will be the vanguard? It must be the members of the Unification Church.

Their faces must reflect the history that was wrapped in worry for the nation, and they must be people who have the scars of the nation’s painful circumstances in their hearts. Because of the Father, we must realize that if we do not leave a legacy of love centered on the Republic of Korea, we cannot fulfill our mission as a nation, and if there is no one to inherit that mission, we cannot be a group that can be patriotic and nationalistic in the heavenly kingdom.

It has been said that the kingdom of heaven begins with me. This morning, please look upon Your children gathered here. If there are those who spend sleepless nights loving others and sacrifice their lives for the nation, shedding tears of effort, please allow us to know that such a group will never perish.

Now the 1970s have come upon us. Blessed families are fighting on the front lines, so please praise their holiness. It is not just about the results of evangelism, but help us to see how precious it is to stand in the bond of following the Father’s inner story and to sympathize with that story. I earnestly ask and desire that You protect their path, surrounding them in all directions.

This morning, I spoke the words, “The kingdom of heaven begins with me.” We must understand that because of one small Kim Amuga, that village honors the Father, and that the county and the nation honor the Father.

The Unification Church must never become a church that meets the sunset in the religious world. If the dawn is not a glorious dawn or a joyful dawn, the members of the Unification Church must struggle not to avoid that midnight.

In the pitch-black world of darkness, if we cannot receive the morning sunlight while solemnly spending the night in alignment with the heavenly principles and adjusting our hearts, we must realize that if we cannot even be a group that sheds tears longing for the sunlight of hope at midnight, we cannot avoid being despised along with our purpose.

May this time be a moment of humbly pledging ourselves before the Father’s heart, and may we discover that we must possess the emotional subject that can add to the kingdom of heaven. Today is a holy Sabbath, so I ask once again that You bless the workers of unification scattered throughout the nation and the world, and protect their paths.
