Heaven begins with me (2)

<Prayer> Beloved Father, Your young children have gathered this morning to bless You, so please look upon us.

The nation that You desire is the nation where our hearts and bodies must go and live. The nation that You must govern is the holy nation that we must devote our lives to and fulfill. The place where You are present is the holy place where eternal victorious lives and all the children who have devoted themselves on this earth praise Your infinite love and serve You forever centered on Your love.

We know well through Your words what kind of sons and daughters You desire in Your heart. Every time we look at all the people of the world, we should be a relative reality and a stimulating existence that praises Your glory, and even though we are a reality that can stimulate joy and praise glory, we did not know how much You grieved when human beings, who were supposed to be the masters, were not before You, and how much You were in a shocking situation.

This morning, please awaken us from our deep sleep and teach us what Your sorrow was from the heart. Even if our eyes are open, we do not have the eyes to look at You directly, and even if our steps are correct, we know that we are still walking with many twists and turns in our steps toward the purpose You desire.

We must run for the will You desire, but we know that we are resentful beings who cannot do so, being in the realm of fallen nature. Father, You know that we have sometimes despaired and sometimes cursed ourselves because we have not always welcomed You into our hearts and have not always cared for You. When we think that You want to care for us with a heart of compassion and love despite our weakness, we realize that both You and we are in a sad state.

How much have You longed to meet those who truly cultivate themselves and appear before You in humility? How much have You awaited true sons and daughters who can stimulate Your heart with all their sincerity? When we think of this, we realize that every time we report our circumstances before You from a place that deviates from this standard, it must be painful for You to face such a son.

We do not wish to host the Father in such a place, but due to the unfortunate ties caused by the fall, every time we reveal our identity in a place of rebellion that does not align with the heavenly will, we come to know the historical resentment and the fallen grievances caused by the sins of our ancestors.

When we think about the fact that we must be nailed to the cross of suffering and the framework of suffering, longing for the last heart of Yours and the bond of compassion, and that we must approach the hope of tomorrow, we realize that if You leave us in such a place, we will become nothing. Therefore, we know that we are a pitiful group that cannot help but report our circumstances before heaven once again.

However, this is not only related to You and us, but also when we see that the group of enemies whom You cannot tolerate, cannot bear, and cannot yield is mocking us through the third point, we come to think of the situation of the Father who must bring us before You even if He hates the enemy. Please allow us, who call upon You from a position of tolerating the enemy, to be accepted.

May our daily lives be such that we can serve You and hate the enemy. May we become sons and daughters who can present a year of such life before You. We must realize once again that we must become those who struggle to welcome a day of joy where we can serve the Father and praise eternal happiness in the place where we dwell.

Father, if there are sons and daughters who want to know what Your nature is like, even if there is someone who represents the poor of the world, they must realize that they are still not more pitiful than You, and if there are those who want to know how much effort You put into humanity, they must understand that even if there is a desperate parent who fights for their children with all their might, there is no one more than You, Father.

Whenever we look at the poor of the nation, we feel that Your heart is present there. In the currents of the world that are flowing, we realize that the whirlpool of Your sorrow has not yet ceased in the painful crossroads that humanity is passing through. Therefore, if there are sons and daughters who struggle day by day, saying that they will not be a source of concern before You, we know that You always want to be with them.

Father, please quietly come and awaken the original self that dwells in our deep hearts. As we reflect on whether we have longed to walk this path with joy and hope following the direction of Your purpose, we realize that we are those who must bear the responsibility of having the justification of such children as we think about living on this earth and then going before You.

Father, You have carried the sorrow of 4,000 years of history from the Adam family, Noah family, Abraham family, Moses, John the Baptist, and the time of Jesus. You have borne the sorrow that no one knows, and we know that You have come carrying it. You wanted a new child to appear on the foundation that was lost, and even if the path of suffering is as high as a mountain before You, who must establish a new nation on that broken foundation, we deeply feel the desperate circumstances of the Father who must move again toward the path of new hope.

“Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as You will.” When we think of the heart of Jesus Christ who offered the final prayer before You, we understand that this is a representative example of how many desperate times there are to leave a victorious faith journey aligned with Your will throughout our lives. When we see that He said, “Not as I will, but as You will,” we can feel the heart of Jesus Christ who realized that human will and Your will are different.

Even if I want to rest, You were the one who had to move forward again, and even if I longed for a moment of comfort, You were the one who had to pave the way of the fierce cross. Even though we wanted to have hope with the earth, You were the one who had to stand in a position of completely denying our hope. Your efforts to save humanity from a position that contradicts this earth with human emotions must have been indescribably great. We must become those who can now sympathize with the circumstances of the Father.

When asking where You will come with new hope on this earth where 3 billion people live, we know that it is not the United States, which boasts of being a cultural nation, nor any other nation. We also know that You will not come to the talented, nor to the educated, nor to those with global renown.

In the shabby appearance that is not equipped, in the poor environment, even in the miserable position of starving, the heart of concern for the Father comes first. Even if there is food, we think again about the circumstances of the Father who cannot eat and wants to present it before You with tears. When we ask ourselves if we have ever had a moment that satisfied Your heart, or if we have ever had a moment that could be remembered before You, we realize that we do not have such stories.

Please allow this time to be a moment to settle and criticize such shameful selves. Father! You are the source of life, the source of hope, the origin of purpose, and the origin of life and death. How much have we served You, how much have we harmonized with Your circumstances, and how much have we had points of agreement with Your motives? You have always been concerned about us while stamping Your feet, but we often fell asleep and forgot our identity.

Every time we think of such selves, Father, the more we long for You, the more we know You, the more we cannot help but expose our sinful facts. We were human beings who had to disappear in despair, giving up all hope for tomorrow, but still, when we think that there is a holy will to awaken Your global hope through such a group, we must once again draw in our hearts how pitiful the Father is, who seeks the highest perfection and the most noble through the inadequate, the humble, and the unfinished.

When at the time of creation, Your holy hand touched a lump of clay, we were able to feel the warmth of Your heart through Your heart. Please allow us to be children who can long for Your hand in the shape of a lump of clay. As we think about how holy the source of the power that made all forms of life from You into one living being is, and as we long for that holy existence of infinite value that You created as an eternal being with Your breath, may we be a group that bows our heads and submits ourselves, determined to run to such a place.

This must be a time to pledge not to tire in taking one more step forward, one more step in pioneering, and one more step in fighting. We are aware that we are a pitiful group disappearing like orphans under the oppression of enemies surrounding us. How anxious You must be, Father.
with a single heart, we hope to pass through this place with determination and resolve. Even if we want to guide you carefully, we have not been able to miss you, and because we have not had relative standards, we have felt the painful and bewildering stories that have prevented us from being guided until now.

Parents who have raised beloved children or older siblings who have cared for younger siblings must have felt the loneliness that seeps into their hearts and the resentment and misery that come from seeing them in a pitiful situation, unable to feed them and facing hardships. The Father, who is the essence of our original heart and nature, must have had so much compassion and explosive feelings when looking at those who are like orphans, who cannot have hope for tomorrow and are in a state of self-denial, wanting to give up. We are a dull group that has not realized that such things continue in our lives and are connected from our past to the present and into the future.

Awaken these people, Father. On the garden of your hopes, let us feel once again that your heart, which wants to inherit your achievements and cultivate the authority of victorious princes and princesses, has passed through us countless times without our knowing.

Now, when we realize that being prostrate before you is a shameful sight, let us have a heart that can be grateful even if we receive your curse and judgment all at once, allowing your good heart to dwell within us. However, since you are not the essence of death but the essence of life, and you are not the essence of the defeated but the essence of the victorious, we realize once again how pitiful you are, being in a position where you cannot abandon us because you remember your name and know your connection.

Now, along with your heart that calls us, let us resolve and unite, so that one individual can become one with the whole, one family can become one with the whole, and one gathering can become one with the whole. When the combined strength of our unity is insufficient to break through all the darkness of death that presses in, let us become those who can overcome and remain by amplifying your power, solidifying our emotional ties and establishing heavenly connections to deliver the final blow.

Today is July 25th. Please remember this day. On this morning, the last Sabbath of this month, remember your children across the nation centered around the Unification Church. Especially those children who are determined to make a new start and are fulfilling their responsibilities in their regions, as well as those who are walking the path of indemnity entrusted to them. I know that those who shed tears of sorrow on the difficult path, as lonely pioneers, will surely not perish. Be with them, and encourage those who are shouldering their missions and working hard on the front lines.

Let us realize that our nation is not far away but is within ourselves, and that our hopes and intentions will not be fulfilled in distant places but must be realized in today's life, moment by moment. Let us feel that we must become a group that can appreciate your dignity within the direct authority of this age. If your will is not fulfilled after informing us once, let us be a group that can instill your earnest heart by informing you twice, ten times, or a hundred times, and remain as a group that shows your desperate appearance.

May your love be with those who are pouring their hearts into their missions, worrying about the responsibilities entrusted to them, as they look towards this place at the end of the age. I earnestly ask once again that the steps of the children present here may not be in vain.

Now, let us have the heart of a hungry child, longing for heaven, and with a heart full of admiration, allow this holy time to be one where we can completely harmonize with your movements and manifest as relative entities.

I earnestly ask that the origin of the victorious heaven, where heaven and earth are unified, may continue from itself, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> I know that there are many religions on earth. These religions claim that they can only be saved through their own beliefs. They teach that by receiving salvation, they can fulfill their desired hopes on this earth.

One cannot possess heaven merely through faith.

Regardless of whether an individual has the highest wish or the lowest desire, one cannot avoid thinking about how to overcome the many paths of suffering and hardship that have not escaped the historical process, nor can one avoid considering how to have a better living environment than others within their own living sphere. We know that we are engaged in our respective faith lives while contemplating these issues.

Today, we are one of those groups. Like all beings, we also strive to develop a new self that is better, higher, and more valuable. We not only hope for something broader and higher, but we also have the desire to unfold that hope on today's stage of life.

When the disciples asked Jesus where heaven is, he said that heaven is in your heart. No matter how good the external relative world may appear, if I do not have the seed of a good foundation within myself, or if I do not have the relative conditions to harmonize with a good foundation, I cannot establish a relationship with it.

For example, when you are in a sad position, no matter how many joyful people are around you or how joyful the circumstances may be, you cannot relate to that joy. To be joyful, I must have something within my heart that can be joyful. Only in a position where I acknowledge that I have an environment in my own living sphere where I can be happy can we feel happiness.

Today, among believers, there are many who hope for the coming heaven. The majority of people believe that if they believe in this way, heaven will come to them. They think that heaven will be connected to them just by believing, regardless of their real life. However, if I do not know the inner workings of heaven and do not have emotional connections in my life, simply believing will not bring heaven into my life.

I cannot feel the essence of heaven merely through belief. It can only be obtained through a life centered on faith or through direct experience of my own. From the standpoint of merely believing, when comparing fallen humans with the unfallen God, the distance is too great. That distance has traversed many historical eras. There are many evils and goods intertwined in that situation. When looking at such humans, even if they go through many paths of suffering, it is difficult to reach the essence of God, and as humans, we cannot shorten that distance. In a one-to-one position, it is impossible to reach God, so faith is necessary to pursue an absolute foundation before the absolute God with all our lives. However, even if I reach the standard of that faith, you must understand that I do not become the object of God's joy.

If there is someone who believes in God absolutely, is that person someone whom God can absolutely rejoice in? No, it is not. It may be a new starting point, a motivation, or a starting point for something that can bring joy to God. However, just because one has faith and absolute belief does not mean that God will like their entire being. Furthermore, we must understand that such a position cannot be a place of complete emotional or situational connection; it can only be a beginning.

That position can only be a starting point for connecting with the world of wishes. Therefore, faith can provide a starting point. The question is how much of a life of practice and experiences we leave behind while believing. The amount we leave behind must be able to connect with the content of heaven; faith itself cannot be that content.

From this perspective, one cannot possess heaven merely through belief. Through faith, one can prepare the connection for a starting point, but when we think about the fact that we cannot present decisive content, it becomes clear that merely believing is not enough. After believing, what must we do? We must practice. We must practice as much as we believe. The practice is the issue.

When looking at faith and practice, believing always comes first; practice cannot precede it. For fallen humans, faith must be strong for practice to also be strong. However, the standards of belief and the standards of practice always differ. God does not desire only faith. He desires the results of better practice and requires faith. Nevertheless, we humans often neglect practice and focus on belief, so we must recognize that we are diverging from what God desires. Is not such a faith life our position?

From this perspective, when we look at the twelve apostles during Jesus' time, they also had such faith. In terms of belief alone, they believed Jesus to be the Messiah who could save the nation of Israel more than anyone else. However, the standard of their faith was only what appeared in the moment. They still had many struggles ahead to reach families, tribes, and nations. The apostles of that time swore to believe in Jesus with their lives, prepared to face death. However, when the time came for them to actually lay down their lives, they abandoned the ideals of heaven and the overall wishes they had through the Jesus they believed in.

If they had had the experience of overcoming such a position through faith and practice, when Jesus faced the fate of the cross, they would not have betrayed him and could have overcome that crisis. However, they thought that believing alone was sufficient to bring about the results of the whole. Thus, a day of sorrow, like a thunderclap, came upon those apostles.

Of course, faith is necessary. However, we must understand that faith is needed only to prepare the motivation for practice. This is why the Bible does not teach that heaven is in believing. It says that heaven is within me. The statement that it is within me does not mean that the subjective position depends on the relative world. It means that I must decide the subjective content. We must recognize that there is a motivation within us humans to make that decision.

In other words, unless we decide on the content that can bring us joy, no matter how much God may rejoice, that joy has nothing to do with us. If God has the motivation to rejoice, then I must establish relative conditions in my own position where I can also rejoice. This is the issue. No matter how much the subject rejoices, if there is no counterpart, that subject will also end up rejoicing in vain. It is merely a desire, and it begins but does not finish.

Isn't that the case in the world? Even if one person has the content that can bring joy, if the counterpart is not in a position to rejoice and is instead in a position of sorrow, they cannot rejoice. When the sorrowful content is greater than the joyful content, the subject that can rejoice must rather comfort the counterpart who is sorrowful. When the counterpart is sorrowful, isn't it our emotional instinct to want to enter into that sorrow and comfort them?

In this light, if God is in the subjective position and we are in the relative position, even if God is in a position to rejoice over us, when he sees us submerged in sorrow, we must think that he cannot help but comfort us from the position of sorrow. Therefore, it is not enough to try to possess heaven with only the standard of believing faith; the question is how to have a practical standard that can correspond to that faith.

This was the question Jesus posed to his disciples as he faced the cross. Knowing that he had to walk the difficult path of death, Jesus could not help but worry about how his disciples would fare. When he said that when he went to the cross, everyone would abandon him and deny him, Peter, for instance, vowed that even if everyone else denied him, he would not. That faith was absolute. However, we must realize that it was only a matter of belief and was far from actual action.

Overcoming difficulties with absolute faith and absolute practice.

From this perspective, we should compare their faith with our faith today. When we consider the intentions we assert as members of the Unification Church and the content of faith centered around the Unification Church, how much of a standard do I have as I walk the path of faith? To what extent do I believe in the Unification Church? Is my belief absolute? It is not. In practicing faith, I am concerned about my own life; the absolute heart is not at the forefront.

When we think about the historical fact that even the apostles, who believed so well and served so diligently, could not join Jesus on the path of the cross, we must ask ourselves if our current level of faith reaches the level of the faith those apostles had. When we critically examine individuals living in the headquarters, do they truly live as those who have passed the standard of Unification Church faith? It is undeniable that they are moving forward based on their own standards of criticism and their own standards of living. It is not a matter of solely pursuing faith; rather, there are many who turn their wishes for faith to the future and live according to their own desires.

When God demands the final victorious authority centered on faith, can we truly take the decisive foundation of victory that God can rejoice in?
The question is whether it can exist. This cannot be a trivial matter. When one thinks that even with absolute faith, God cannot fully present heaven to me, today in our faith, centering on one’s own faith, saying, “With my own conviction, I can go this way,” can such a faith truly realize heaven? This is indeed a significant issue.

We, who are in a habitual and detrimental decline, trying to prove ourselves and rationalize ourselves under the guise of pursuing the will, are in a position similar to that of Satan, who used tactics to evade before God. When we consider whether we can truly replace God and maintain a firm foundation, it becomes a matter of great concern.

When we look at ourselves, is there heaven in my heart? How many people can confidently say, “I have heaven in my heart”? If there is someone who possesses heaven, regardless of who they are, they would want to belong to that very place. If someone has realized heaven, any living human being, regardless of being a descendant of the fallen, would want to easily attain that heaven, which is the point of hope. Anyone would want to go there day and night. They would want to go together, live together, and suffer together. Wouldn't heaven be a place where one would want to suffer together and die together?

The presence of sorrow does not cause separation, nor does the existence of pain create a crossroads. Even if one faces difficulties, that place cannot be divided. If the position of possessing heaven is one that can overcome death and all hardships, then no matter what difficulties or paths of suffering the person who possesses that heaven faces, it cannot block their way. Heaven cannot be present where there are conditions that can obstruct it.

To realize heaven, various issues are currently presenting themselves as practical problems on the path of the will. If one is not in a position that possesses the content recognized by God and is hesitating in front of the direction they should go, then heaven cannot be a place where they can dwell. How you resolve and overcome these issues is an urgent matter.

Before swearing to heaven and deciding to go for the will, the primary issue is to discover whether I am a necessary and appropriate relative entity that heaven requires. You must understand that it is more necessary to be someone who asks, “Is heaven not necessary for me?” than to be someone who confidently presents, “I am not in need.”

It is more important to be someone who can explicitly state before God, “This is my relationship with You,” rather than someone who asks to be recognized based on their prestige, face, and the length of their faith. Only then can it be proven that heaven is in that heart, and that one can affirm being together with heaven. A person who does not possess such content cannot be considered someone who has a relationship with heaven.

So, when you place the vast will before you, or when you place the will that God desires through history before you, how seriously are you united with that will? Are you practicing absolute faith centered on that will? Even if the wind blows and storms rage, even if I die and perish, I must have the unwavering conviction that “this belief is certain. If I am wrong, I am wrong, but the will is certain.” It is exceedingly foolish to envision heaven while possessing a faith attitude that differs between morning and evening.

If there is a way to approach heaven, what kind of way is it? What kind of way must it be? There will be no way to heaven from a position of self-concern. Once one realizes that they are far from heaven, they must break down their self. Only by attacking oneself can a path to heaven, or even an indirect heaven, be opened. However, if someone is in a position where they simply defend themselves, trying to adapt their relative environment to themselves, placing themselves in a subjective position and pushing forward against the relative environment, that person will not be able to establish a relationship with heaven.

As today’s title states, heaven begins with me. No matter how complete the relative heaven may be, if I cannot respond when that heaven calls, I will have no connection with it.

What kind of place is heaven? Is it not a place that overcomes Satan? It is not merely a place where one has overcome oneself. It is not just a place where we have overcome our own selves today. Heaven cannot come to a social environment, a fallen world, or a habitual environment where Satan reigns. Because Satan dominantly controls this habitual environment, and since Satan dwells here, heaven can only come after overcoming this environment of Satan. Heaven is established in a place that is contrary to the contents of the world of Satan. Isn’t that so? If it were not, it could not be heaven. Even if it is called heaven, it would merely be a deception to mock the environment.

Therefore, the concept of heaven can only be established in a place that has overcome Satan, in a place that denies all factors that Satan can confront, not only denying but also settling those factors. Heaven can be affirmed only on a foundation that has negated and settled all historical relics or all aspects of life that remain under the negative conditions of Satan. Without leaving such conditions, one cannot present the content of heaven.

Heaven is such a noble place. It is a heaven that speaks of a standard that can align with absolute criteria, yet the concept of heaven that we envision today is far too chaotic. We are longing for heaven from a very corrupted standpoint. While it is certain that heaven will arise from overcoming with an absolute faith standard in this living environment, it cannot determine the origin of heaven by that alone. Heaven will unfold only after overcoming Satan, who has troubled God for thousands of years and has deceived countless humanity.

It goes without saying that heaven cannot be realized merely by believing passively. It cannot be realized with just a believing heart. Since Satan always presents challenges, heaven can only be realized by overcoming the path of struggle. However, there must be sovereignty here. Additionally, there must be many people. Many families must come together within a nation or national system to establish a comprehensive system for a single purpose.

From this perspective, God’s position requires that we can harmonize and act together without conflict, in any time, environment, or place, with the subject. While one may feel the heaven that dwells in their heart when they are prepared to dedicate their life and believe, the actual heaven has not been realized on the stage of reality even after paying the price of countless martyrdoms and sufferings over 2000 years of history. Heaven is not something that can be established so simply.

How serious is the statement, “Heaven begins with me”? When we consider this phrase, how serious is the position of this “me”? How much does it represent an absolute position for us humans? There is a verse in the Bible that says, “You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might.” The term “Lord” can be recognized in a position that has an absolute content that cannot be forgotten for eternity. Heaven does not come from believing in the Lord your God; it comes from loving the Lord your God. Isn’t it through love that the Father’s will is fulfilled? It is not through belief but through love.

From this perspective, we must understand how inadequate our faith has been and how far we have been from reaching the principles. There may be someone here for the first time, but one cannot attain a position where they can receive comfort centered on the individual. Just because heaven is realized in your heart and God is pleased with you as an individual, does that mean it becomes heaven? It may become an individual heaven, but it cannot become the whole heaven.

From this perspective, what God desires is not an individual heaven. He does not take joy in a heaven that an individual has established and possessed. Can we say that heaven has been fully realized just because one person is pleased? God sought to connect all nations horizontally centered on one person, Jesus Christ, whom He sent to this earth, to seek the whole heaven. That is why He sent the Messiah to this earth and sacrificed Him.

Considering this, in our faith today, can anyone stand with an absolute limit and declare, “This is absolute for me. Who can take this faith away from me?” before heaven and earth? We are those who do not even possess such faith. God is guiding and leading us, nurturing us spiritually through our prayers and our hearts at every moment. When we consider God in this light, we must not think that He is nurturing us comfortably. He does this because He believes in us absolutely, believing that if He does this, there will surely be a reward. It is because of this absolute faith that we continue to work hard, even if we face setbacks or losses, believing and believing again. Before I absolutely believe in God, God has already believed in us absolutely.

Therefore, when we, who are under the dominion of death, try to take a side road, God blocks and guides us from that path. When we consider this fact, it is not because God loves us. It is to discover a certain aspect of faith. It is because of the belief that the value of that faith can manifest as the sons and daughters of faith that He longs for us. Because we stand in a position where we must believe in humanity, even if we are frustrated several times, He helps us. Is it because we are likable? We must think about this as believers today. The fact that God stands in a position requiring absolute faith from us already indicates that He believes in us.

Additionally, there are times when God makes humans experience certain things. During the course of our faith life, if we have experiences we have never felt before, some may think that it is because they have put in effort and that God has an obligation to respond in kind, but that is not the case. Even though the absolute God has made countless saints and prophets pay the price of blood over 6000 years, heaven has still not been realized. When we consider that God is still in a position where He cannot meet His beloved sons and daughters, thinking that God has given me grace because He likes me is a misunderstanding. It is because we must manage and stabilize such groups while looking forward to tomorrow’s hope that He helps us. That is unavoidable.

However, if I think that grace is given because I am likable, that is a grave misunderstanding. When we see people who have spiritual experiences, some become arrogant and confident. The more they do, the more they should feel their shortcomings. I have seen many people say, “It’s because the environment is wrong, not me…” Such people do not have a long future ahead of them.

That is why Jesus rebuked the Pharisees. The Pharisees were arrogant. While they seemed to be equipped outwardly, they were not equipped inwardly. They were already in a high position internally. They thought, “I can represent the nation.” To represent the nation, they should have gone through the historical process of sacrifice and possessed all the relative conditions that God worked hard for, yet they were in a position where they could not do so and claimed, “In this era, I can represent the nation.” When we look at these issues, we must recognize how contradictory our faith life is today.

Therefore, heaven cannot come without overcoming the “me” that I desire today. Heaven will not come if I leave even a few things that are the cause of my desires, in other words, if I leave the content of desires that can be motivated from me. From whom must the desire start? Not from oneself, but from the other or from the will. It must start from the will. A motivation that comes from oneself cannot become heaven.

Heaven is realized from the point of denying oneself. From this perspective, the teacher himself cannot help but be concerned about the Unification Church today. Is the will the motivation, or am I the motivation? I must not be the motivation. However, today’s humanity often places themselves as the motivation behind the will. The will demands a path of suffering, but the “I” seeks to betray that. It is a contradictory position. The will says to go to the right, but I want to go to the left. People present conditions like, “How much suffering have I not endured since joining the Unification Church?” to justify themselves.

Those who try to justify themselves cannot enter heaven. Absolute faith is not a place for self-justification. One must stand in a position of being justified. There is no content of any presentation there. It is a position of being justified. Even if one has done well, they cannot say they have done well. Even if I can acknowledge something 100 percent, to God, it is one. What I acknowledge as 100 is one to God. Therefore, one cannot seek heaven from a position that presents oneself.

Where does heaven start? It starts from the point of absolute faith. Absolute faith is not something that can assert oneself. That position is one of absolutely denying oneself. Without standing in a position of absolute denial of oneself, absolute faith cannot emerge. Do you think absolute faith will emerge when you go down the path of faith while positively affirming worldly matters?

When we look at the fundamental issues today, most people wake up in the morning, eat, and engage in habitual living while saying, “I am confident before God.” Many people believe this way. Such people cannot possess heaven. They cannot be confident. Without any relative factor that recognizes me, one cannot have absolute faith standards.
is. If you haven't even established an absolute standard of faith, how can the heaven that can be realized only after overcoming that absolute standard of faith be achieved? It's impossible. Why? Because Satan resides in that place.

The motivation for your life comes from heaven. The motivation for desire also comes from heaven, but it is paired with Satan. It is stained. There is more black than white. Therefore, the path of pioneering faith is not a path that can be sought based on any of your own concepts. Among those who have entered the Unification Church and know the principles, there are not many who think about the principles. They may think they are in a position to inspire others by lecturing on the principles, but anyone can speak. Speaking is easy for anyone. However, practice is difficult. How deep and high is the background behind the words? You cannot measure that based on your own standards. In our faith life, what kind of thoughts do you have regarding emotions and daily conduct? You are always establishing yourself. This is the most important thing in the world of faith...

When Jesus prayed while carrying the cross, saying, "Abba Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will," he did not pray from a position of confidence and dignity. Saying, "Not as I will, but as you will," was to open a way to plead on behalf of humanity, knowing that heaven was a fate that could not be returned to once it was reached. He prayed such a prayer knowing full well that it was unlikely to succeed. If Jesus had prayed such a prayer to avoid the position he was in, he would not qualify to be the Messiah. He prayed such a prayer, risking his dignity, knowing that it was a path he had to take.

How much work must humanity do in following the path of the cross that Jesus walked? He prayed not from the position of a son who receives God's love but from the position of one who does not receive God's love, to establish the authority of a son who helps the Father while bearing the titles of an unfilial child and a sinner. When thinking this way, Jesus is a grateful figure. If Jesus had prayed out of fear of death centered on his personal self, he would not qualify to be a complete offering for all humanity. He would be less than Isaac. Isaac remained silent when his father took him and bound him to the altar to sacrifice him. He disregarded his own situation before God even before going to the place of death. When thinking this way, one cannot complain. Humanity is always lacking, and thus cannot face God from such a position. To establish a relationship with God, one must be recreated. Therein lies the problem.

True Faith
Because of being in such a position, we have not been able to establish heaven even with an absolute view of faith until now. We could not even start the journey to heaven. To achieve heaven, one must first establish self-governance. Whether you are eating or going somewhere, your daily life must be conducted in conjunction with God. You are an object being before God, not the subject. You must have a heart like that of a wife serving her husband and like that of a child serving their parents. When you move, it is like reporting to your parents, saying, "I will go here and do this." You cannot have a life of faith apart from living directly with God.

Today, the Unification Church says you must be a filial child, a loyal subject, and a virtuous woman. This does not mean to take an independent position. It means to acknowledge the relative self before the absolute self. That position is not a place where you can openly assert any opinions you may have regarding your own perspective before the absolute self. That is different from democracy. It is not a place where you can assert whatever you want.

In the pursuit of heaven, there can be no self. There can only be sincerity and overcoming. After finding heaven, there can be a self, but in the position of seeking heaven, there can be no self. The democratic way will not work. There cannot be conditions under which one can assert oneself. As long as such conditions remain, that world is under Satan's dominion. Fallen actions undoubtedly create a world of Satan. The fallen world is undoubtedly under Satan's authority. There, society or the world is formed based on the bloodline relationship of Satan, and all factors of Satan are intertwined and contaminated. It has become one lump. It is stained with the blood of Satan. Such things must be completely eradicated or entirely overcome.

Therefore, in the path of faith, there can be no self-assertion or self-concept. Absolute faith means a faith that leaves no self-concept remaining. Isn't that right? When one says they believe absolutely, there should be no factors that absolutely oppose their self. In the desire to become one centered on God, there can be no self-assertion. It must completely align with what the subject demands. To be in complete alignment means there is not even a single thought of self-assertion.

If there is a place in your faith life where you can assert yourself, that place is not heaven. A place where you can wish for things as you please, no matter how well you believe, is not heaven. You must think seriously about this fundamental issue. The person speaking here is also thinking seriously about such issues.

When does heaven begin from me? At what point can it start from me? Heaven is not limited to just me as an individual. If I have established a joyful heaven in my heart, how do I apply that joyful heaven to my family? This is not a trivial matter.

For example, according to the principles taught in the Unification Church today, first, one must overcome the first cross. Overcoming oneself is the first cross. Next, one must overcome the second cross. The second cross is when the husband and wife, or the family, align with the will. Overcoming the second cross is harder than overcoming the first. You must understand that. This is also true from a principled perspective.

When humanity fell, it was not just the individual who fell. Adam and Eve fell as a couple, and not only the couple but the family fell as well. Therefore, the restoration of the son-in-law is not simple. Both individual perfection and the perfection of the counterpart must be achieved, and the right of good reproduction must be formed. Thus, in order for my individual self to overcome myself, I must bear the cross. I must walk the path of the cross.

A snake cannot grow unless it sheds its skin. To shed its skin, it must push its way through the gaps in rocks. The opposing force must be applied to the body to shed the skin. The forces of darkness have become one with our blood and flesh, and how can we shed this? We cannot follow it. Therefore, wisdom is needed. We must go entirely in the opposite direction. To completely shed, we must go entirely in the opposite direction.

Material Subject - The First Problem Fallen Humanity Must Overcome
From this perspective, one must go to a position where one can absolutely deny oneself. Why does a person have worldly desires, that is, material desires? It is because of the fall. Because of the fall, we lost material things, and because of the fall, we lost our counterpart. Then, because of the fall, we lost our subjectivity. These three are the problems. Broadly speaking, these three are the issues: material, love, and subjectivity; these are always the problems.

Is material a problem in front of you? When I want to use a fortune for a purpose, even if there are people who object, they cannot accuse me. "That money is mine..." they might say. Is that really their money? This is how material accuses us. "Hey, where is the reason for that money to be yours?" It is God's property, yet having fallen into the realm of the fallen, it should not be claimed as one's own. The material accuses us. Therefore, the issue of material... Then there is the issue of heart. What is the greatest enemy on the path of faith? It is money, money. The Bible says you cannot serve both God and wealth. Money is the problem. So how do you capture money?

The teacher also has a lot of interest in money. Money is necessary. For the purpose, one should be able to spend all their money. One should use what is saved for something more valuable. This is the issue.

You should not be dragged by or constrained by material connections. When there is food, one should not think of eating first; that is not right. In that regard, these days it seems different. In the past, when people went to the army, they often missed food. When going to prison, it can bring tears. You do not realize how serious it is to eat.

What do you use to evaluate the standard of character in front of the whole? You evaluate it by observing what actions a person takes when they are hungry. When someone is in a hungry situation, if they show signs of being hungry and act recklessly, no matter how much they are the sovereign of that country or the spiritual leader of that nation, they are failing as a leader. However, even if a person lacks character and education, if they can exercise self-control and overcome their hunger, they can become the leader even in a prison cell.

When I was in prison, a famous pastor from a certain region came in with his son-in-law, who suffered from fever. This disease causes high fever at the same time every day. Despite having fever medicine, the pastor did not give it to his suffering son-in-law. He exchanged the medicine for some porridge from a third party. Such things happen in prison. Each action of that pastor can destroy everything he has cultivated in faith until that point. In that place, material determines the entire value of character. Thus, a small piece of material can determine the entire value. Material is frightening. Isn't that right? If ten people live together and one wants to dress better than others, will they get caught or not? If one wants to eat better than others, will they get caught or not? Will they be liked or disliked? They will be disliked. This already falls under the conditions of accusation. Therefore, eating, dressing, and living are bait in the world of Satan.

I am currently driving a car, but the Lincoln car gifted by my American family is still in a warehouse in Busan. Should I drive that car or not? There are many concerns. If I were like the world, I would show off and boast about it. However, I would rather sell that car and buy a church in the local area. If I drive that car and show off, I will get caught. That is bait. It is Satan's bait. If you see good bait and say, "Oh, how nice," and pick up a spoon, you will get caught.

What I have learned from having good teachings is that even when receiving a meal in prison, if there are no side dishes, I did not complain, saying, "I am the leader of the Unification Church, and there are many members who eat better than I do." While eating plain rice with just water, I called out to God, saying, "Weren't you the one who came out with hope for tomorrow?" Even if there are side dishes, they cannot be eaten together with rice. In prison, there are nearly a thousand people eating, so soup and rice cannot be served together. You have to eat within an hour, and soup is served from one side, while rice is served from the other side. Therefore, it is complicated. It takes 30 minutes just to get rice. Once you get the rice and soup, the meal time is over. And as soon as meal time ends, you must leave for the work area within three minutes. You have to go out and work.

So, there is no room to eat with one hand holding soup and the other hand holding rice. You eat whatever is available. Soup is served in one line, rice in another, and you eat as it is served. If you get rice first, you eat the rice. You eat plain rice. I learned how to eat plain rice there. Plain rice is really delicious. I have always liked scorched rice, scorched rice. I think God trained me well. The taste of scorched rice I used to eat is the taste of plain rice. As the burnt flavor adds a bit more, it becomes so tasty that the taste of plain rice is nothing compared to it.

I always ate soup with soup and rice with rice. Even in such a situation, I was prepared to dedicate my life centered on the purpose and to fulfill my duty of filial piety and loyalty to God. But to complain about food and side dishes? When I see such people, I feel a fire inside.

Even if one lives in a bad house, God provides a better house. However, some leaders, in the current situation where it is difficult to buy a house, have obtained a good house while going into debt of fifteen thousand won a month or so. What will happen to that child?

I am indifferent to my living situation. I have always cut off the material aspect. I become a debtor. I receive reminders from my mother several times a day, saying, "Since life has become like this..." Shouldn't I pay back whenever I can? Yet I do not pay back immediately. You all need to think about this issue. Material is my enemy. Before overcoming this, if I possess wealth, I cannot walk the great path. I cannot walk the original path. The teacher is someone who completed this training in their twenties. Therefore, when there is a command from heaven, I abandon everything, including my children, and leave without hesitation, carrying only my bundle. This is how the Unification Church began.

That is why material is the enemy. If something good is there, one should not think of eating it first. If a table is set with side dishes, there are people who think, "If someone eats one piece of meat, I will eat two." Such a person is already failing. Satan draws a red line there.

Even when fleeing, it is the same. I brought Wonpil here, but everyone is hungry. It is not that I do not want to eat; it is the same for everyone. The teacher might be different, right? Not at all! The teacher knows hunger better. A person who has experienced hunger knows the taste of food better. When living in a refugee situation, when food is prepared, you pick up the spoon together. But who puts down the spoon first? The person who puts down the spoon first becomes the leader of that situation. It is certain. The person who puts down the spoon first becomes the owner. Just wait and see if that is true. 

Among the daughters-in-law who have married into a family, if there are three sons, which daughter-in-law earns the most trust? It is the daughter-in-law who picks up the spoon last while managing a difficult household.
I hope it's not like that. Ladies, if this statement is wrong, please protest to the teacher. Not just protest, but demand a severing of the neck. It is certain. If there is someone who gives away all their nice and beautiful clothes and lives in the worst clothes themselves, that person will become the owner before long. Isn't that the case with our Unification Church? The teacher has endured some hardships. You all have endured a lot too, right? But still, you feel empowered, don't you? That is our foundation.

I am currently living in a two-story house, but my conscience tells me this: my faith until now has been to build a house for God. That is the fundamental principle. You must pray. The teacher is absolutely not haphazard. The big issue is that it’s not done alone. It’s done in cooperation with heaven. Do you understand? I don’t even talk about this to God. Only those who are in spiritual communication know about it; the teacher does not. The teacher walks a path to build a bridge of undeniable truth and to teach with a proper framework. So if you just follow the teacher, you have nothing to worry about. Do you understand? “Yes.” But if you receive something good, you must recognize it as good; otherwise, it means your eyes are darkened. 

However, when comparing the valuable global foundation established by Jesus Christ and his disciples and countless Christians who walked with the blood of unjust martyrdom over the past two thousand years, you are those who have received heaven’s blessings on an even greater foundation. Is that right? When you listen to the words, isn’t that the truth? “Yes.” Do you feel that it’s the truth? “Yes.” If you feel that way, you should search day and night. If there’s an old man at the door, you should grab his hand and weep with a serious expression that doesn’t exist in the world. Even if the old man is eighty years old, you should treat him like that. 

When you cross over the hill into a neighborhood, think, “When I cross this hill alone, there will be someone waiting for me at the top when I come back.” If you visit at night, there should be at least one or two people waiting by the fire for the church leader to arrive. If you don’t do this, you will become lonely in the spirit world. Are there such people here? There, everyone gathers, eats together, sheds tears together, and prays… This is the path of restoration, this is the environment of joy, and this is the foundation. There must be people who are determined in their hearts to create such an environment. 

Is there anyone among you who thinks of the teacher? How many times do you think of him in a day? If there’s anyone who thinks of him at least once a day, please raise your hand. You must be honest. Do you think the teacher doesn’t know? The teacher is not like that. The teacher does not feel that way about you. The teacher cannot be indifferent for even a moment. 

When I am tired and try to sleep, I find it even harder to fall asleep. “Oh, I’m tired today, so I should rest.” At such times, I feel even more sorry, “Why have you become such a pitiful God? I have time to sleep out of the 24 hours, but haven’t you been ruling the spirit world for six thousand years without a moment’s rest?” When I feel that I am the son of the one who has tirelessly taken on the miserable history, I often find myself unable to cover myself with a blanket, praying until I fall asleep. 

When I wake up from such sleep, I am startled. It’s night here, but isn’t it day in the west? “At this moment, isn’t there someone in the east who, taking the name of the teacher, is risking their life to go to heaven?” When I think of these things, it’s overwhelming. The teacher does not live according to his own will. 

That’s why I try not to be in emotional debt. As long as I have this heart, those who resent and curse me are not good. You must unite with the teacher and invest your sincerity like the teacher. Among you, there should be those who, regardless of the season, want to bring even a piece of meat to the teacher, crossing mountains and rivers, even if it rots. There should be people who come with tears. I don’t want to eat meat for my own sake. If you don’t do that, it means you are stealing what I have taught and guided you. 

You should have faith with the heart of a child. Then you will receive. So what has the Unification Church leader done wrong until now? It’s different from you. That’s why when I’m lonely, when I’m weary, when I’m incredulous, I may not receive human comfort, but I do receive God’s comfort. Shouldn’t you be like that too? That’s how you develop. 

We must understand that we carry a heavy mission in this tremendous era. Do you understand? “Yes.” We carry the mission of the three eras. Therefore, the question is whether we fulfill our responsibilities in this era or not. This path has taken six thousand years, so we cannot cut off even a piece of that six thousand years of arduous journey. In the moment I blink my eyes, in the moment I breathe, I must act. That’s why the question is how much can I see the necessary victory points centered on heaven in this moment with my eyes, my mouth, my hands, and my body. 

When God is busy, when God is urgent, and even when there are difficult matters, I must be in a position where God can consult with me. When I am in difficulty, does God know? And when God is in difficulty, can He call me without hesitation to discuss? Am I in a heart posture that can respond without hesitation? Do you understand? When the teacher asks you to do something, do you struggle to fulfill your responsibilities through the night, thinking that you will carry the difficult cross alone? 

If there is someone who lives with that mindset, pledging their global responsibility and the responsibility of this three-era mission centered on the present moment, that person will surely become a son or daughter of God. Whether in the Unification Church or in the local community, they will inherit that traditional history, and such a person will become a responsible leader who can guide future generations correctly. You must understand this. Do you understand? “Yes.” Our mission is immense, and the stage we stand on is correspondingly large. This is the reality we face today. 

Moreover, the time we have to establish a relationship with the teacher is not long. It has now come close. Knowing this, we must bring about a new revolution by coming here this time. We must re-examine ourselves more critically. We should look in the mirror at our own faces, squinting our eyes and asking why our eyes look like this, why our mouths look like this, if our mouths are for eating? What are these ears for, and what is this body for? We must critically examine these things. 

I hope you will be those who fulfill your responsibilities on the foundation of the realistic providence that must prosper through tears, blood, and sweat.
