Joyful Retreat
People living in urban areas are lacking in wisdom. The air is bad… Moreover, the more cultured a person is, the less they want to live in the city. The bad air makes them sick.

Construction of International Cities and Retreat Centers
If we take Washington, a developed country like the United States, as an example, over 75 percent of the population is Black. White people all live around the outskirts of the city. Some commute from as far as 100 kilometers away. If they drive at 100 miles per hour, they can arrive in about 48 to 50 minutes. There are people living at a distance comparable to that between Seoul and Daejeon. Do you understand? We have entered an era where people commute from such distances. Therefore, people living in the city are lacking in wisdom. Korea will also see such an era in the not-too-distant future. It would be better to live about 20 minutes away from the urban center rather than in housing areas centered in the city. That distance is quite interesting and peculiar.

That is why we are currently developing this area, but in the future, we plan to clear all the surrounding mountains and, as quickly as possible, create a recreational area in this beautiful region of Cheongpyeong by August 13, 1971 (Friday).

Once everything is built and there is nothing more to add, we will create a highway. We will build a bridge from outside Cheongpyeong Dam, connecting the mountains to this place with a private highway. Then, even if we tell everyone to go elsewhere, they will not want to leave. We will gather everyone here at once, allowing us to earn money, conduct retreats, and achieve dual benefits.

In the future, we will make it so that anyone who does not come here will not be able to avoid it. Once we create an international village here, it will become a place that everyone wishes to visit at least once. In this way, we will earn money, conduct business, and carry out various activities.

We are also in the process of acquiring the former residence of the head of the intelligence agency, and we are purchasing the mountain behind it. Once that is done, we will have technicians install a cable car from here, making this place very attractive. There has been a saying that this will become the New Seoul, and we are trying to create a new Seoul here.

Yesterday, I spoke to our Japanese members about this. When I asked who would build the village first, they said, "Japan will build it first." If Japan builds it first, they will end up last. (Laughter) Upon reflection, that is indeed the case. Even if the first builders do well, those who build later will use that as a standard and will be able to add something to it, ensuring they build well. So, I asked, "Would you still want to build first even if you end up last?" (Laughter) We are planning to create such a place.

We will establish a highway and create an international village. If we can keep people here for about a year, those who have visited will have a stronger sense of national identity. We cannot allow that to happen, so next, we will build comprehensive apartments where people from a hundred countries can live. We will then conduct a lottery and establish a three-way connection, allowing them to live in those apartments for about three months before leaving. We must create such a global apartment complex. We need to prepare everything so that even Europeans can live here comfortably.

How long will our Korean people continue to live by farming? We need to live leisurely. Do you all want to work? Do you want to work or not? "We don't want to work." Even if you don’t want to, you will have to. This means the time for farming in Korea is coming to an end.

So, what will happen in the future? The number of Unification Church members will continue to grow globally. Germans have come and gone, and now the Italian leader is here, but in the future, if people from Europe do not visit Korea, they will lose face. Those who have come and gone will boast about it. This will lead to competition among everyone. If only important members come and go, those who cannot go will find themselves in a situation where they lose face. For Unification Church members, it will become essential to visit Korea quickly to maintain their dignity, leading to rapid promotion.

As this happens, things will get busier. Even now, our headquarters is quite busy. I have no time because foreigners are coming and going. Japanese people are lining up, singing "Nilliri Dongdong." If this continues, there will be hardly anyone else traveling through Gimpo Airport except our members. When that happens, we will take them to all the scenic spots within a two-and-a-half-hour distance. We will show them the beautiful mountains and rivers of the eight provinces, and a two-and-a-half-hour bus ride is sufficient. Three hours would be tedious. If we connect these distances and give them a tour, they will realize that "Korea is truly a place that God cannot help but love."

Once we send them back, they will return to their countries and boast about Korea. This is how we will attract many foreign tourists. When relatives of Unification Church members travel through Asia, they will have no choice but to visit Korea. We will utilize that situation. We will contact hotels everywhere and create a 40-day itinerary, allowing them to tour around.

By doing this, everyone will owe us a favor, so we must do things our way. We will plan everything and incorporate the principles into it. In this way, we will promote our Unification Church to those people and even evangelize our relatives. We will spread the word that Korea is a better tourist destination than countries like Switzerland.

In the 1960s, the teacher walked a 21-day course. You all know that, right? We will have Japanese people retrace this path. "This 21-day course was traversed by the teacher during the time of persecution, riding in a bumpy jeep along mountain paths, so since this is a holy site, you must walk barefoot." They will walk barefoot. We will have all the Japanese people line up and start walking, then start again at the next location, and wait to start again… If we do this, people waiting in the mountains of the Korean Peninsula will fill the paths. When Japan finishes, the next will be America, creating competition among them. Those who are impatient will say, "How can I wait here?" and will come early to wait. We must understand that the time will come when the teacher will have them walk barefoot along the paths he traversed. Do you understand? "Yes." You should be grateful that you are walking this path now without taking off your shoes. Do you understand? "Yes." Such a time will come. Just wait and see.

When I visited the Jerusalem Temple in Israel, the museum director said, "It would be nice to have even a broken piece of metal that Jesus used during his time." If such a thing exists, they would not trade it even for America. That is the reality. When you go to Jerusalem, it's amusing. The contents of the 66 books of the Bible, including Zion and David's city, are all within a 20-mile radius of Jerusalem. The situation is quite poor. However, when you see Christians visiting Jerusalem, they walk carefully and seem to be in a frenzy, feeling as if they have entered heaven.

Seeing that, it makes me wonder how wonderful Korea will be in the future. Also, isn't it true that pilgrims of Islam are continuously visiting the desert areas? If we consider that, Korea will become even more magnificent. Therefore, we must ensure that Korea thrives and prospers. To do that, we need to create tourist attractions.

If we create an international village here, who will be the manager? It cannot be the people from each country. So who will it be? In the future, families will come here to take responsibility and manage it. Therefore, families will naturally have to live in good, high-quality housing.

And since the managers will all be families, they will be like living cultural assets of the Unification Church. Families have a history centered around our Unification Church history, so they must teach the history of the Unification Church to the pilgrims and guide them. They must teach how individuals should live and how families should live, and they must unravel history. Such a time will come in the not-too-distant future.

As for the land we have purchased so far, we have bought less than 900,000 pyeong. This means we have only acquired one-fourteenth of it. Do you understand? However, among the land visible here, over 80 percent is ours, as it has good location conditions for building villas. Therefore, the amount we have invested so far is equivalent to the cost of purchasing about 13 million pyeong of land in the mountains. Once we establish this, our hundred-year plan will be realized.

And these mountains are all famous mountains. In the future, we will create canals by digging tunnels in the mountains so that boats can navigate. On both sides of the banks, we will have cars running, and we will build hotels next to them, creating beautiful underground hotels along the riverbanks. We will ensure that everyone must pass through here at least once, charging high prices for entry and exit. In the middle, we will build an elevator, allowing people to go up to the observation tower and enjoy the view. Do you understand? Such a situation will unfold here.

Stories about Building the Retreat Center
Originally, we did not plan to build a retreat center here. We intended to set up tents to use as a venue for pastors' public hearings. However, when it rained, it became muddy and miserable, which was quite frustrating. I bought three tents and set them up, but I realized that if this continued, the Unification Church would have to go through another round of restoration and suffering. (Laughter)

Initially, we planned to start construction around the end of July or the beginning of August, but that wouldn't do. I listened to the weather forecast through the broadcast and learned that the rainy season would start in mid-July, so if it rained and the ground became muddy, it would be difficult both inside and outside. So, we had no choice but to say, "Let's start from July 2." We began then. We worked until July 10, but it took an extra two days for painting. So, the construction period was ten days, but it was as if we built it in eight days. We held the public hearing on the 12th, so we had to finish by then, painting on one side and doing whatever we could to avoid embarrassment during the public hearing. This is how we proceeded to hold the Principle Research Association meeting, followed by the high school students' meeting, the professors' seminar, and you all are the fifth group. Do you understand? "Yes."

If any of you came here for the first time and wondered, "What is this?" those who have participated until now would complain. So, do not have such a mindset. The people who worked hard to build this house are now sitting at the back, and if anyone dares to complain, they might grab you by the collar. "What is it, you brat! Are you a man sitting comfortably like that? We have worked hard and sweated!" And someone there! The person with the darkest back, take off your clothes! Show us the first place winner! Turn around! (Applause) There is no separate black person. Do not think that black people are only those in distant lands. If you are exposed to sunlight all year round, you become black; it is nothing special.

There are many interesting stories about building this house. We built it in eight days, and by the 10th…
If we don't build it, we won't be able to inform any reporting team. So we have to finish it by the 10th, but why does it keep raining? That damn rain is an enemy. It keeps pouring down without stopping, and are we supposed to just fall over and say we're going to build a house? That's a big problem. We were planning to make a workers' camp here, but since the roof is covered, the rain leaks in, which is embarrassing. And we can't even use a tent; what can we do? 

So, when it comes to building, we have no choice but to be stubborn. Also, the land here was all mountains. The only place we had for land was where the teacher had set up a small tent, and there was only a spot as small as a snake's tail. We had to dig all of that up and fill it in to build a house, so think about how complicated that must have been. 

And we needed to bring in materials, but the boat broke down at that time. That's the work of Satan; that damn boat was out of order for about two days. When I contacted them to bring the slate, they kept saying, "Yes, yes," but they didn't bring it. They said they would bring what we needed for tomorrow tonight, but what did they actually bring? I was so frustrated that I was running back and forth, and around 9 PM, I negotiated for a special boat to come and load the materials, and it arrived here at 1 AM. At 1 AM, after unloading everything, it was already around 3 or 4 AM. The boatmen probably thought it would take that long to unload all the slates. But when I went to get the boat in the morning, all the slates were gone. (Laughter) They thought that since it was raining and the slates would get wet, they must have covered them temporarily. But guess what? No one went up to the roof to hold them down, and the slates were just sitting there. So when I looked closely at the slates, I found that all the nails had been hammered in. That's why this house is called the "Goblin House." (Laughter) 

Now, to build a villa here in Cheongpyeong takes about three years. Usually, it takes a year and a half. Do you think the local people will help us build it? They come with a pickaxe and when it's time, they just shake off the dust and leave. Do those people want to work diligently? They are people who are good at cheating people from Seoul. 

When I had the locals come to build the retaining wall, at first, they were just loafing around. Watching them work made my eyes sore.... To them, I looked like the boss. Out of face-saving, I pretended not to see. But after a few days of working hard, these people automatically received training. When I looked at the young people, I would say, "Okay, let's go up on the roof and put up the slates." They would quickly become good at putting up slates, and when I said, "Let's make a katsuoki," they would quickly become carpenters, and when I said, "Put the veneer board and hammer in the nails," they would do it perfectly. They became proficient at everything. The young guys who thought it was a joke realized that this was amazing. So they received training automatically and went on saying, "Oh, this is scary." (Laughter) 

In just two weeks, we built it all. A house like a villa came out in a week. It looked like we were building a house, and when I came back the next week, there was an incredibly wonderful house, and professors, pastors, high school students, and college students all started flocking in. So it was quite contrasting with the surroundings. 

When you say "Cheongpyeong," it becomes a headache for the intelligence agency. Why? Because the bourgeoisie from Seoul come here with their luxurious boats and build all sorts of villas, showing off. This is that kind of place. But since the Unification Church bought the land, they thought the Unification Church would build villas too, but instead, they quickly built a training center. And since university students and professors come and go at the training center, rumors spread. It's contrasting. It's like hitting without saying a word. 

By setting this up, even if we bring in airplanes in the future, they will forgive us. Right? We can say this is for the training center. The security chief of the Gapyeong Police Station and the intelligence chief came and gave speeches, so now it has spread throughout the military as the International Victory Federation Training Center. It is also supposed to be reported to the central government. So everything went according to our plan. Even when we sing praises here, they will think we are singing the International Victory Federation song. (Laughter, applause) There is a villa of Mr. Lee Hu-rak, the chief of the intelligence agency, here, but even he can't show off while riding a boat with his friends. So it turned out very well. While they are having fun, we are conducting education here, so they can't make a fuss. 

And if a lot of people gather like this, what happens? The locals will think, "The Unification Church is building a house here, so the land price will go up," and many people will start dreaming. However, if we come here making a lot of noise and riding boats day and night, it will be impossible to build villas here. (Laughter) 

At first, the land price will go up, but if after a year or two it doesn't go up, the land price will go down. So that kind of strategy is necessary. 

In total, building this training center cost about 4 million won. However, when you consider the land price and all other aspects, it will absolutely not be a loss. We have completed a hastily built structure. 

What kind of house is this? When people living in other villas come and see it, they say, "What kind of goblin house is that?" (Laughter) This is that kind of house. Everyone is receiving training here. Behind this, there are many stories you don't know. There were many nights when we worked overnight in the rain. Sometimes we worked until six in the morning. "Okay, eat and sleep." And when you try to close your eyes, "Wake up!" So there was never a time when I could close my eyes. That’s how we built this house. 

Precautions to Observe During the Training Period
You are the church leaders from the local areas. You are the church leaders, right? "Yes." You are not just church members; you are church leaders. Do you understand? "Yes." You are not dead bodies; you are living people. So you must know this history and be trained as church leaders. You should not come here and start acting up or wanting to take a bath from the very beginning. If you take a bath, it will be a big problem. Why? Because this is a dangerous place, famous for being so in the Cheongpyeong area. Do you understand? If you go in to take a bath, you will end up in trouble. 

This is a dangerous area. The water depth here is 70 meters. The water coming down from Gapyeong or Hongcheon collides here and flows out, making the water flow very complicated. Therefore, the water temperature is not consistent. The surface is warm, but as you go in, the temperature difference can be several degrees every meter, which can cause heart attacks. 

Not long ago, I had some university swimming athletes come here and told them to swim over there, and in the middle, they were like, "Oh, oh, oh!" They were good swimmers, but in the middle, they lay down and said, "Oh, oh!" At first, I thought they were just playing, but then I saw they were sinking. So I pulled them up and asked what was wrong, and they said the temperature suddenly dropped, causing their nerves to become numb, and they couldn't move their legs. That's the kind of area this is. Do you understand? So if rumors spread that "the church leaders went to have a training retreat in Cheongpyeong..." it would be unpleasant. What if something happens? The temperature difference is severe, so you must be especially careful. Do you understand? "Yes." Absolutely no swimming. 

Next, don't think, "This is our dock and our boat, so I should try it. If I don't, the boat will cry." You can tell at a glance. Do you understand? Because if something goes wrong, it will be a big problem. This is a tourist area, so the people from Seoul who want to have fun come here. They don't want to ride boats when many others are riding; they want to ride at night when it's exciting. They want to do what others don't do. 

Since they like that, if there's a boat in front, they will say it's okay as long as they feel good. And by night, they usually have a drink. Their eyes become bloodshot, and they think it's okay as long as they feel good, so they often crash into diesel engine boats running alongside. Do you understand? If it’s dark and they crash, do you think they will know? They won’t. Do you think the person passing by in the boat will know there are people there? Fortunately, if the person riding the boat has a light on, they might see, but…. Because of such people, it is truly dangerous. If a big accident happens and the boat capsizes, no matter how well you swim, you will faint there. If a boat collides and capsizes, a fast-moving boat will crash into it. So if a boat comes rushing in and crashes, it will be a big problem. "I swim well, so..." Not at all! It doesn't work that way. If an accident happens on a dark night, fear will take over, and you will forget about swimming. Weak thoughts will come to mind immediately. Do you understand? So it is very dangerous. Absolutely do not ride boats at night. Do you understand? "Yes." If you listen well, I will take you on a motorboat ride later to show you around. If you really want to ride, connecting a drum to push back and forth instead of a boat can also be fun. (Laughter) So don't ride boats! What else? "No swimming!" 

Then you might think, "Now I'm feeling down." You might think, "I came to Cheongpyeong to have fun, but this is all messed up." You might feel down, but instead, we will make sure you eat well. (Laughter) Do you understand? "Yes." If you sweat sadly, you might not know the joy that comes with it. 

Next, what should we do? We need to reflect. Looking back, the church leaders have not taken responsibility. Do you think you have taken responsibility? Reflect on it. In the 1970s, did we fulfill our responsibilities before the standards that heaven requires? We need to critically reflect on this. Do you understand? "Yes." 

I will try to come here as much as possible when I have time. So you need to reflect. And we will pave the way here. The teacher plans to go abroad soon. During that time, I will let you know what needs to be done, so everyone should put in their best efforts. That's why I brought you here. So you should recognize that this period is important and spend it meaningfully. 

Look around here. You will realize that this place is really nice if you take a walk around. I traveled around the world last time and even climbed to the top of the Swiss Alps, but there is no place like this. Anyone who comes here will say the same. 

Act with new hope 
Last time, I brought Sasakawa here to show him around, and when he returned to Japan, he said that the Unification Church's Teacher Moon has foresight. While others are busy building churches, he praised the way we buy land, saying it shows different thinking. In fact, when he came here, he found it really nice. 

As the world’s fortune is about to sprout anew, it is significant for you, the church leaders, to come here, unite your hearts, and embark on a new journey before heaven. Considering all these things, I gathered you here, so I hope you will work hard to achieve the intended purpose of gathering here. Do you understand? "Yes." I will buy the land.

The Value of Blessed Families

The fall was caused by individuals, specifically by a man and a woman, but it is not limited to just one man and one woman; it possesses historical and cosmic significance.

Because this is the principle, we can see that the history of restoration until now has been carried out through a history of recreation. Thus, the act of subduing Satan is not done solely by ourselves. When we establish the conditions of relationships that allow us to stand in the realm of perfection without falling, and when we stand in a position that absolutely values God, since Adam fell in a position where he did not absolutely value God, when we stand in a position that absolutely believes in God, God recognizes that we are standing in a position better than Adam and Eve, and He intervenes to create a foundation where we can confront Satan. Then, God will act with His original heart and inject powerful strength into us, allowing us to have a second conviction to stand boldly against Satan, which means that Satan will no longer be able to confront us and will be subdued.
That is why emphasizing unconditional faith today is not for the sake of unconditional salvation. The attitude of faith in today’s established churches is that if you believe unconditionally, you will be saved. While that statement is correct, the fundamental difference lies in what you must do with that unconditional faith. You must fight and win against Satan. Only then can you achieve salvation, which today’s Christians do not consider. They think, “If I just believe, I will be saved.” There is a fundamental difference here.
So, what does it mean to say to believe unconditionally? What does it mean to have absolute faith? It means to stand in a position that has the conditions to surpass the standard of not being able to believe in the absolute God and not being able to unite with God, which Adam had when he fell. Only then can God act upon that person and prepare the foundation to subdue Satan. Only after subduing Satan and establishing the standard of victory can one enter the Kingdom of Heaven.
However, even today, established church faith believes that regardless of whether Satan exists or not, if you just believe, you will be saved. You must understand that this is a fundamental difference in faith. Even if you believe unconditionally, you must subdue Satan to achieve the purpose of salvation, and only with the results of victory that subdue Satan can you go to the Kingdom of Heaven; merely believing unconditionally is not enough.
From this perspective, ultimately, the question is how to establish a standard that God can cooperate with. The call to believe unconditionally is because humanity has fallen so much that God cannot relate to us, so by having faith, we can at least rise to a symbolic absolute standard that is not fallen in our hearts.
However, today, our purpose is not just to establish a symbolic absolute standard before God, but we must establish a substantial standard. In other words, we must become an absolute being before the absolute God, not just a symbolic one. There is a difference in words. If God is the absolute being, then we must become the absolute being in relation to that absolute being.
So, what must we do? What kind of position is that? It is a position that transcends faith. It is a position that has subdued Satan. Is that not so? Who can slander in front of the absolute God, and who can confront the absolute God? There is no one. That is why no one can slander a person who stands in the position of an absolute relative being before such an absolute being. Who would slander a person who stands in the position of an absolute relative before God? Even in worldly examples, who would dare to say anything to a woman with a husband? It is the same.
Today, the members of the Unification Church must stand in the position of an absolute relative and an absolute being. If you stand in the position of having an absolute substantial standard, just as Satan cannot slander before God, Satan will also not be able to slander before you, and the Kingdom of Heaven will unfold on earth. Is that not so? If there are conditions left for Satan to slander, the Kingdom of Heaven cannot be established. Rather than the Kingdom of Heaven, there is a fight that must be fought to establish the Kingdom of Heaven. Since there is Satan that destroys the Kingdom of Heaven, there is a fight left to subdue that Satan; it is not that the life of the Kingdom of Heaven remains. Is that not so?
Therefore, what must we do to establish the Kingdom of Heaven on earth? We must become an absolute substantial being, and just as Satan cannot slander before God, we must stand in the position of practitioners who cannot be slandered by Satan, even while living on earth. Only then can the Kingdom of Heaven be established. Can the Kingdom of Heaven be established in a position of fighting against Satan? That position is one where you fight to establish the Kingdom of Heaven; it is not a position where the Kingdom of Heaven has been established.
We receive cooperation from God centered on God. Even when you pray, you say, “Father! Please cooperate with me,” right? You pray to receive cooperation. Is that not so? There are stages to receiving cooperation. Just because you joined the Unification Church does not mean everyone is the same. From a heavenly perspective, there are stages like rebirth, growth, and perfection.
So, who would God want to cooperate with the most? It would be someone who, once cooperated with, does not feel the need to cooperate again. God is looking for someone who can be the last through that one cooperation. Wouldn’t that be so? He does not want to keep giving and giving and giving… He wants to cooperate in a position where, after one cooperation, it becomes the last, and the work that can be demanded of humanity before God is finished. That would be the purpose of God’s desire to cooperate with humanity.
From this perspective, if we quietly think about the path of restoration, being in the position of a servant of a servant...
Would God want to cooperate with humans just because He wants to? This is the issue. What do you think? Would He cooperate because He wants to, or would He do it because He doesn't want to but has no choice? "He has no choice." You know that well. He cooperated because He had no choice. 

Why? To reach the day when there will be no need for cooperation. It is unpleasant and distasteful, but God is leading humans, who are in the position of the servant of servants, with the responsibility of restoration, in order to meet the last time when God can truly seek cooperation. 

To quickly escape the position of the servant of servants, 

Would it be better for the position that God dislikes to continue for a long time, or would it be better for it to end quickly? "It would be better for it to end quickly." Think about it. Answer clearly. Would you prefer it to continue for a long time, or to end quickly? "It would be better for it to end quickly." You would feel the same, right? Everyone, think quietly about God's position. Wouldn't you want the position of the servant of servants to be decided quickly, so that the period of being a servant of servants could end in just a day or an hour? Absolutely not.

If you end quickly and still carry the label of a servant of servants, it means nothing. Isn't that so? That is being a servant of servants.

"The ten-year painful path." Once they understand this, it is the less intelligent and foolish people who take the quicker path. Those who blink and think about various things, weighing their options, and trying to find a way to go without effort will fall behind. 

Bears are incredibly stubborn. A bear climbs a high mountain, carries a burden, and has to suffer to sleep there. Otherwise, they abandon that place and go elsewhere. How stubborn and foolish is that? 

Foolish people have followed God's will. 

This applies to the people of the world and to you as well. Even when looking at the providence of restoration, it is evident. Think about Grandpa Noah. How foolish was he? Was Noah a foolish person or a wise person? "He was a foolish person." He was so foolish that there could be no one more foolish than him. God, who is omniscient and omnipotent, told him to build an ark. Wouldn't it have been better if He had told him to build it by the riverside or in a plain? It would have been easier to carry wood, and it would have been easier to work morning and night. No matter how you compare it, building it on a mountain is worse than building it by the river. Who would think, "God is less capable than me"? Would anyone think that? How can you believe in a God who is less capable than you? You should believe in a God who is better than you, right? However, believing means believing regardless of whether He is better or worse than you. Believing in God is that. You believe before you experience it, not after. Right? You believe whether it’s good or bad.

In Israel, it wouldn’t take me five hours to make a round trip.

The Heart of a True Leader
You should think that wherever you go, you are going with the universe, and wherever you go, you are going with heaven and earth, and that you are not going alone. You need to have such conviction. Even when eating, you should not think, ‘In the past, I used to eat meat with rice, but now I can only eat a bowl of porridge with water.’ You should have a standard of expectation. Even if there is only water, that is a standard of expectation. Centered around water, with eyes, mouth, and God, that is a standard of expectation. This is the way to think.

Even if there are no side dishes, just placing the spoon and chopsticks allows you to establish a standard of expectation centered around God. The items you pick up through that standard of expectation are not bad just because they are bad. Do you understand? Are they bad or not? They are all good. “I only like beef and dislike beans.” Is that so? If that’s the case, you become someone who only likes the top of the universe and dislikes the bottom. If you only like white rice, can you be the owner in the kingdom where only white rice is eaten? Can you? You need to be qualified to do so, and to be qualified, you need to eat. You cannot know without eating. If you don’t eat, you won’t know. So you should be able to say, ‘Oh, barley rice is delicious. One bowl of barley rice is better than ten or a hundred bowls of white rice. I am the king of barley rice. I only know barley rice.’ You need to find that position.

If they still dislike it, say, ‘Try living two days without it.’ If they still dislike it, then three days, and if they still dislike it, then four days, five days… Keep them fasting. (laughter) If you say, ‘This is a universal remedy,’ everyone will want to eat it. That is a remedy better than any universal remedy. Among the remedies for blessings, such a remedy is the best. (laughter) That is what I think.

Let's think about "value." Because I am a valuable being, the possessions I have acquire objective value. This is the principle of creation. When the subject appears before the object, the subject and object interact and become one. Isn't that so? The object also receives equal value rights from the subject. This is the teaching of the principle. Therefore, a person who neglects the possessions belonging to them cannot last long. They must love the possessions that belong to them. From a single piece of paper to all household items, everything that belongs to them must be regarded as precious. It goes without saying that they should save.

Effective ministry and evangelism
How should one evangelize? If you want to evangelize a certain girl, how should you do it? You should become a trustworthy church leader who can say that it is okay to take that girl away by visiting her parents who listen well to her. You should prepare a deposit of around 300,000 won to bring her, and if her parents allow it, you bring her to the church to serve and evangelize her among the congregation. Can you always keep that girl with you? When girls are about to get married, they are in their teenage years, and their hearts are somewhat fluttering. They want to wear pretty clothes, see things, and taste things.

So, on market days, when this girl says she is going to the market, that is when you execute your plan. First, you contact a member who has already been evangelized to let them know that a certain girl is going to the market. Then, while she is walking in the street, you arrange for her to meet someone who can talk to her. "There are many people in the Unification Church I attend. I feel grateful to God for this and that. I was moved by this and that when I joined the Unification Church." You share your story of how you came to walk the path of the Unification Church. That is how evangelism happens.

You must carry out indirect operations like this. You cannot rely solely on worship times. Think about it: if you are active 24 hours a day, through all seasons and in all directions, will you not develop? Will you develop or not? "Sermons are only on Sundays," and then on Sundays, you think, "Where should I look in the Bible? Let the hymns come out, let the choir come out." (Laughter) That cannot be the case. Do not do that.

When people laugh, some laugh weakly with a "heh heh!" while others laugh robustly. There is a variety of expressions even in laughter. Some laugh with "hee hee!" while others laugh with "ho ho ho!" and some with "ha ha!" There are all sorts of people.
Rolling, going down, slipping, falling, bursting...
It's the same with the eyes. Even when blinking, everything is different. Try to find if there is even one person who is the same. They are all different. Among your friends or church members, some have certain personalities, and others have different temperaments... Just by looking at someone's face, you can tell what kind of mood they are in. How interesting would that be? (laughs) Such people exist. Those with such impressions will be the subjects of the teacher's research in the future.

If you peel off the eyelids, they may all look the same, but when the eyelids are on, they are all different. The pupils move around; when happy, they look like this, and when crying, they look like that, right? (making a face) Eyes are all different. It is not easy to recognize someone just by looking at their eyes.

So how do you know that? You think about what kind of environment a person with certain eyes has and develop a method to select people with those eyes. Do you understand? You select someone with eyes like a certain person. You can also select based on ears, nose, and eyes. They all resemble each other. By observing such things, if someone has a kind appearance, and if three out of ten traits match, you can conclude that the person is at least 50% similar. There are only four features on the face: eyes, mouth, ears, and nose, and if three of them are the same, it means more than half is a match. You can discern whether the person is good or bad based on that.

You study with such criteria. You are also providing research data to the teacher right now. To roast like this, you also need to know how to buy sweet potatoes. Which sweet potatoes are delicious? Sweet potatoes grown in sandy fields mixed with sand or stones that drain well are sticky sweet potatoes. They are really sweet. Try eating them. Is it tasty or not? However, sweet potatoes grown in muddy fields are completely different. If you boil them, they become mushy. It's like throwing boiled sweet potatoes from the second or third floor. (laughs) If you boil them, they become like that. You know by looking. If you rub the skin with sand, you can tell if it's sweet or what it is... And it must be firm. It shouldn't be smooth. It should be bumpy but without hair. The skin shouldn't be thick. These sweet potatoes are really delicious. You need to study all of this. You will know by eating a lot. (laughs)

If you find out which house in a village has the best sweet potatoes and buy a few sacks when they are cheap, you can eat them until spring. If you have to eat sweet potatoes, even if you have to borrow money, you buy cheap and delicious sweet potatoes. If you have one sack of delicious sweet potatoes, you can survive for a month. If you prepare like this in advance, you can eat sweet potatoes for a year without dying. Do you understand? You must know that gaining weight from eating sweet potatoes is also a blessing.

Everyone, when you first eat sweet potatoes, they are really delicious, right? Am I wrong? Let me tell you about the first time I ate sweet potatoes. There were no sweet potatoes in my village. However, my maternal grandmother's house was 20 ri away, and when I went there for the first time, I saw sweet potatoes for the first time. They called sweet potatoes "ji-gwa" there, meaning "earth fruit." I later learned that the original name is sweet potato, so I called it sweet potato, but at first, it was "ji-gwa," the fruit of the earth. Ah, when I first went to my grandmother's house, they gave me that, and I thought, "What on earth is this...?" While wandering around my grandmother's house, I saw vines spreading out, and when I asked what it was, they said it was "ji-gwa." "What is ji-gwa? I've never heard that name before. How do you eat it?" They said you dig it up and steam it. "Is it like a fruit? Can you pick it? Can you dig it up now?" I dug a hole and found a few roots coming out. Since I pulled out the sweet potato vines, could I just leave them there? (laughs) I asked them to boil it for me, and when I ate it for the first time, oh, how delicious that sweet potato was...! So I decided to eat it all by myself and sat down with a basket of sweet potatoes. Sweet potatoes go down so easily. After eating them all, I was full. Feeling good, I thought we should plant them next year. I intended to plant them the next year, but I couldn't, and it was three years later that we finally planted sweet potatoes at my house.

From the following year, whenever it was sweet potato season, I would run 20 ri every few days in the evening, saying, "Mom, I'm going out for a bit." I would go eat sweet potatoes. When my mom asked, "Where did you go?" I would say, "I went to play." Playing meant going to my grandmother's house to eat boiled sweet potatoes. (laughs) That taste was really like honey.

What was so delicious back then, why does it taste different now? It’s because people have changed. It’s not that sweet potatoes have changed; it’s that people have changed. Remembering that time, I think, "Oh, sweet potato, I used to enjoy you so much, but either I've lost my affection for you or your taste has changed; it must be one of the two!" I pick one up and taste it, and it’s just not the same.

Aren't you the same? You roast sweet potatoes, wrap them in paper, and place them on a shelf to eat after a lecture or when you feel curious. If you leave them there, no one will eat them. After a sermon, you hold a cup of water and munch on sweet potatoes, thinking, "Who came today...?" That feels really good. When you eat and think, all your thoughts are about family.

You must live joyfully, focusing on various issues or your own life. Why live with a frown? If you do, even God will run away. (laughs) If your fate is such, if you were born with that destiny, then while living, don't have a sad face; instead, have a joyful face and live with a smile, singing a tune while looking at the garden.

If a leader of the Unification Church lives like that, rumors will start to spread in the village. Our sons and daughters absolutely cannot live like that. Naturally, their heads will bow down, and even while walking, they will walk weakly. No matter how poorly you live, no matter how much you starve, you should sing a tune. Sing popular songs that the village kids like, and when the moon rises, look at the moonlit garden and sing moon songs; when it rains, sing rain songs; if you're in the countryside, sing rural songs. Buy a record and play hot songs when it's hot and cool songs when it's cool on the village microphone, and if the workers start singing along to the tune, the villagers will have plenty of good things to say. 

If you put your heart and soul into it, anything will help you.
A person must know how to create an atmosphere. You shouldn't always have the form of someone who can't live just because you are poor. If you don't have clothes, borrow a friend's clothes, wear a red tie, and go out early in the morning. When the villagers ask, "Where did you go?" you say, "I went somewhere." That will pique their interest. What’s wrong with meeting the county head? (laughs) It’s about changing.

If you get to know the county head like that, you can invite him to your village. When the county head comes, you can say, "As you can see, we live like this. But don't despise us just because the Unification Church has no money. I am younger than anyone else. In ten years, I might be above you!" jokingly. "The ideology of the Unification Church is to rise from the bottom, and our Teacher Moon's ideology aims to instill self-reliance and independence in young people, so when building a church, we could have built a brick house, but we started with just one tatami mat. I have only been here for a few months, and this is just the beginning, so don't worry about starving today. Although we are small now, who knows how big we will become in the future?" You can casually talk like that, and within five minutes, you can maintain your dignity and more. Do you understand?

If you are hungry in the evening, go to the county head's house and say, "County head, I came to get dinner. At my house, it's dark and there’s nothing to eat, so I'm starving to death. But your house is bright and has a lot of food, so I came. Please treat me to dinner as a passing guest." Then you receive a meal that the county head personally prepares for you. What’s the point of living miserably while doing a good anti-communist lecture? You can do it like that once a week.
Next, on birthdays, you send birthday greeting cards. You need to send them three days in advance. Do you understand? If there are about 360 houses in that neighborhood, you write down the birthdays of all 360 people when you go to give a lecture. Then, three days before their birthdays, you send out all the birthday greeting cards. If you send a birthday greeting card and still don’t hear any news, you go visit them. (Laughter) If it’s Mr. A’s father, you ask if he received the birthday greeting card you sent, thinking today is the birthday of Mr. A’s father. You say you were passing by and couldn’t just walk by after sending a birthday greeting card, so you stopped by for a moment and ended up enjoying the birthday feast at their house. You live your life like that, enjoying the year as if it were a fresh play. To do that, you need to research how many houses in that neighborhood hold celebrations centered around their sons and daughters. (Laughter) Such houses are well-fed and well-off, so you can find out about them. Then, you can spend your goodwill and visit any house without making them feel uncomfortable. That’s why you also need a relative like Kim Sat-gat. “Sleeping on the mountain peak at sunset, Mr. Moon.” (Singing, applause)

To restore history, sometimes you have to act like an actor, sometimes like a beggar, go to a gambling den, and do all sorts of things. If it can contribute positively to your purpose, it’s not a bad thing. In that sense, the teacher doesn’t feel guilty even when singing pop songs. Do you understand? It’s not that I do it for anything in the world. By fostering such feelings and through the emotional circumstances, if there’s a way to contribute positively to the heart of restoration and provide more stimulating impressions, wouldn’t that be wonderful?

The teacher loved music during his youth. Our children also love music, especially when we play stereo music in the car while going somewhere; they jump around non-stop until we come back. These kids feel good, and if they stay still, they get bored. Seeing that, I realize they take after me. (Laughter) They get happy just by keeping the rhythm. They have a talent for that.

I was like that in the past too. The owner of the boarding house I lived in was a gentleman who drove a car, the eldest son of a well-off family in Gangwon-do. About 30 years ago, he was quite a man when it came to driving. He had traveled everywhere in the country. He knew all the folk songs and had hundreds of records. So, I devised a plan to win over the landlady. I greeted the owner and every evening brought in the dinner. If the landlady asked me to do something, I would do it, fulfilling all her requests. This was my strategy. Following this plan, within a few days, the landlady was completely smitten. She even said she would like to have me as a son-in-law. Of course! Then she brought all her records to us. (Laughter) We listened to all those records. I would bring a few at a time…. Even when the owner came to check, I wouldn’t get caught. After listening to all the records, I would change them out and listen to them all. “How many of those records did your owner listen to? Did he listen to them all or not?” I didn’t have to be better than the owner. I said I would listen to them all within a few days and kept them playing 24 hours a day. I even played them at night while I slept. (Laughter)

Singing well is truly wonderful. A filial child sings while patting his mother’s back, and young men and women sing about their feelings for each other, entering that realm. As someone who takes responsibility for restoration and leads the way, shouldn’t you achieve your desires somehow? This is all the way (道). It’s the realm of the way. The people next to you know this. This is how you stay up all night. How do you sleep? When you sleep, you keep it on low and listen while using the blanket. I remember those thoughts. I’m that passionate. When I do anything, I don’t want to lose to anyone.

You should also learn to sing. I have never formally learned to sing in my life. I’ve never learned to sing through a teacher. I don’t want to do that either. I prefer just to listen and sing. If I want to do it, I do it. Singing is necessary.

When you observe the environment and it’s a time when you have to hold everything in your hands, you need to do such things. Going through various trials and difficult situations is a necessary preparation process to achieve that one purpose. Sometimes, you might even have to sell yourself off wholesale. What I mean is, when this neighborhood is losing to that neighborhood in a wrestling match, I go out to support this neighborhood. You do that when it’s tough. You go out, plant a flag, sing, and take the leading role at that time. You must take a keen interest in all sorts of things and experience them with determination. That’s how I am. When I go to a gambling den, I don’t just want to pass by; I want to try gambling. When I see a fighting group, I can’t just pass by; I have to step in and resolve it. I hate losing at anything. I dislike losing in fights the most. When I see something wrong, I have to catch it or do something about it; I can’t just stand by and watch. I want to try everything.

As I go through life like this, I realize that all of it is for the purpose of achieving that one intention. If you do everything with your heart and soul, it won’t be a minus for you; it will be a plus. This is proven through the teacher’s experiences.

Live actively. 

Even when the teacher was in prison, being beaten and tortured all day, even when they tightened and twisted him with a piece of paper, he would say, “Let’s see what you got, you guys.” And he endured. The detectives would say, “I’ve been a detective for several years, but I’ve never met someone like this.” They would say, “Oh, we’ve met the wrong person.” Of course! (Laughter) Even while being beaten, I felt good. I like that kind of thing. I dislike trivial matters. I’m active. You all need to understand this.

You, who are following such a teacher, must also become such people. Otherwise, you won’t catch the teacher’s eye. He dislikes those who just watch and are cautious. Since your teacher, who guides you, has fought like that until now and has established a tradition through such experiences, you must understand that you need to do well. Do you understand? “Yes.”

That’s why you should learn in advance about that village. When you meet an 80-year-old elder, you should try saying something like this: “Grandfather, you’ve lived here for a long time, do you know which mountain has which rock, and what’s what?” If that grandfather replies, “I’ve heard of such things,” then that grandfather should learn from you. You should investigate and know everything about the surrounding nature, “Who planted that willow tree….” Then, if you know more than the older people in that village, you can say, “Oh, grandfather, you’ve lived in this village for 80 years, but don’t boast just because I’ve only lived here for a year.” You can hit him with that. Even if it makes him feel bad, it’s still valid. He can’t ignore you.

It’s the same when you go out to work in the countryside. The teacher is very good at planting rice. When you see people planting rice, they all say, “Hit it. Pull it. Drag it.” But that’s not how it’s done. Our Pyongan-do Jeongju region was the most developed agricultural area in the country. The Japanese even set up an experimental farm there. Since the Jeongju region has a climate comparable to that of Hokkaido, Tokyo, and the Ohu region, the Japanese established it as the most exemplary agricultural experimental site at that time. They implemented the fastest farming methods they researched as a demonstration case for all the citizens.

When planting rice, if you draw a line at a 90-degree angle on both edges of the field, it becomes the correct direction. When planting seedlings, you first stretch out the line. Then, from the edges, two people enter each row to plant the seedlings, ensuring that seedlings are planted where there are no footprints. If you plant seedlings where footprints are, it can lead to big trouble when heavy rain comes. There’s a turning point, and the two of them plant following their footprints, going in and out. Therefore, they don’t fill in while going back and forth along the seedling line. How much longer would it take to plant seedlings like that?

If one person decides to plant twelve seedlings each and competes with others while planting well, one person can plant over 500 pyeong in a day. Two people can plant over 1,000 pyeong. If twelve people are lined up to go out together, the slow ones will naturally fall behind. Such people cannot work in that village. If the top worker in that area can do twice as much as others, rumors will spread that he can plant twice as much, and he will be sought after anywhere, even for double the pay. Why? Because when planting rice, having a few such people is essential; they help others plant well by following their lead. This is also a competition. For a week, they gather men from several villages to compete. Then, they quickly finish the work of several villages. This is how they study farming methods.

When pulling seedlings, you must hold the root well to pull them out easily. In a group of ten people pulling seedlings, they form a team, and when it’s “Team A,” they designate who pulls the seedlings, who moves them, and who ties them. When pulling seedlings, you must split the roots well. You need to grab the root part firmly to pull them out easily. When tying the pulled seedlings, you shouldn’t tie too many; you should only tie as many as you can hold in one hand. To do this, you need to study. Because of the competition, you can’t help but research. (Recording pauses briefly)

Collect various materials, research, and work hard.

To become a true leader, as mentioned earlier, you must have the heart of true parents and set up internal and external strategies on the stage you are responsible for, digesting that stage through internal and external strategies. To do that, you need to collect various materials, research, and work harder than others. Whether that village is drawn in or not depends on what kind of stimulus you give to the people in that village and how you leave plus conditions for them. Who would like to owe someone? “No one.” Even the teacher doesn’t like such people. You must clearly understand this. Do you understand? “Yes.”

Next, the church leader, who takes on the responsibilities of parents, is what kind of leader, and how does he take responsibility? Furthermore, how do you establish a relationship with God? The question is how you relate to God. You must devote yourself. You must devote yourself. That’s the issue. As a leader, to pray all day long, you must long for God more than you long for people. The heart of admiration and longing must never disappear. You should feel a yearning that is indescribable, like a hungry child wanting to nurse. At such times, in a way that no one knows, quietly and subtly, you receive spiritual nourishment on your own. Others don’t know that.

It’s the same with mothers. Mothers think the teacher doesn’t pray. Since she lives downstairs and I live upstairs, she doesn’t see me praying. She thinks I go upstairs to sleep, and when I come down, I’m just waking up. I pray as much as I usually do and then sleep. The teacher lives that way. Being a Unification Church teacher is not an easy task. You must pray. You can’t decide on big issues alone. Do you understand? A country can fall, and when the providence of restoration crosses a peak, and waves crash over, you must be someone who can bravely overcome it by building up sincerity.

When you have to decide on a new significant issue, if you make a mistake, the country could fall. If you make one mistake, the Unification Church could also fall. Standing at this crossroads where the Unification Church could either fail or thrive, you must do whatever it takes to establish the heavenly nation. Do you understand?

The church leader must not let tears dry up.

Everyone must decide for themselves. Therefore, you must have your own secret methods. No matter how much opposition there is, if you follow that principle, it may seem impossible, but it will work. Even if there is something opposing, you must push forward and show the results that align with God’s will. To do that, you must be able to judge based on internal issues and have the cooperation of heaven. To receive the cooperation of heaven, you must devote yourself.

The church leader must not let tears dry up. Who is the truly pitiful person in the world? It is the church leader. The church leader is someone who always carries sadness. When thinking about God’s heart and the time of the providence of restoration, there are many times when you feel pity for God. When considering what to do to walk the path of restoration, when you think, “I can’t help but take this path because of who I am,” you often feel a heart-wrenching sadness that can choke you. There are many times when you feel like you could faint. At such times, you often find yourself holding onto the world or someone passing by to gather yourself. Without such a heart, one cannot do God’s work for God. When passing through the neighborhood and seeing something bad, you think, “I may pass by now, but I will come back and clean it up with my own hands.” This is the kind of life you lead.

If there is a God standing in such a position, how much must that God suffer to restore this world? Therefore, you must pray a lot. Do you understand? Without prayer, you cannot receive God’s compassion. You cannot receive God’s help. The sorrow that comes to you is because there is no background of compassion centered on you. That’s why you feel sad. Isn’t that right? If you become someone whom God can have compassion for, you will not be lonely. You will never be lonely. Even if you lie down in a cold room or a room like a block of ice, you won’t feel sorry for yourself. There is a complex content in that.

That’s why didn’t Jesus pray a lot? Don’t our Unification Church members know how to pray? If you don’t have time to pray, pray while walking. I’m telling you to pray while walking. Instead of praying, you should evangelize. You should evangelize in place of your daily prayers.

What kind of person is a leader? A leader is someone who gives. A leader is not someone who receives. When giving, you must give something new, not the same thing. You all find it difficult to preach, right? You can just follow the principles.
However, preaching is difficult. This is because one should not give the same thing. Isn't that right? One should not give the same thing. Just as parents must carefully choose what to feed their beloved children, one should not give the same thing.

If you have nothing to give, you must receive from God. You feed your family with what you have received from God. Isn't that right? Discussing with God... Ultimately, you are clearly representing God. 

There are times when you pray without knowing what you are praying for. At such times, while praying, you are moved by the words you are saying. When you pray from such a state, the audience becomes captivated before God, and they come to realize that "God is the driving force of life and the essence." When people have such experiences, they come to feel that God is absolutely necessary. To connect these stories and captivate the audience, prayer is absolutely necessary.

The great people of the past, those who are mentioned in history, are not all great scholars. A great person is truly someone who feels the hunger of the heart. When their heart is full, they can feel joy and enter a state of ecstasy, and the audience becomes captivated by that. You must understand that.

The Path of a Leader
You must give, but to give, you must receive. Where do you receive? You may receive by listening to the teacher's sermon at the headquarters, but when you are alone, you must establish a way to receive from God.

To do that, you must cultivate your abilities. You are not going alone when you go out. You must receive revelation. You must go with the heart that you are with True Parents, with your mother and father, and that the world is judged by you. You must have the heart that what is before you can influence God's providence, and wherever you go, you must go back and forth as a shield of judgment. If you go back and forth with that heart just three times to accumulate merit, it will become a turning point, and you will naturally come to realize that when you go, God goes, and when you come, God also comes. When that happens, the place where you stand will develop. Do you understand? How many hours do you pray each day? You must pray even if you don’t sleep.

A Leader Like True Parents
Returning to the point, what kind of leader should you be? You must be a leader like True Parents. Then what? You must pray and strategize. After that, you must spread the truth. You must understand that these are the important tasks of a leader. Where do you receive? From God. How do you strategize? By learning God's strategy. You learn God's strategy and create the best strategic plan.

Then, since I have taken on the responsibility of a leader, I must have the conviction that I am the sole responsible person who cannot be infringed upon, and that the position I stand in is the position of True Parents. In carrying out strategies in harmony with God, the first thing you need to know is the heavenly law. This is what I am telling you based on my experience, so try to practice it as it is. I am asking you to see if it is true or not. Do you understand? "Yes." If you do that, without a doubt, the places you go in the future will develop. If you live like that and then depart, many family members will follow that path, and if you move to another place, they will shed tears for you, and not only shed tears but will also come back and forth to where you have moved.

If such a situation arises, when person A moves and person B comes in, the family members may go to where person A has moved, leaving person B behind, and there may be jealousy towards person B. Those who are jealous cannot become leaders. They must learn from that lesson. For example, if a leader responsible for evangelism in church A goes to church B, and even though a new leader has come to church A, if the members of church A all follow that leader to church B, then that leader is an excellent leader. Do you understand what I mean? At that time, the trusted leader of church A should not stop the members of his church from going to church B. He should let them go cleanly.

He should go to church B, learn how to lead, and then play the role of a servant. By playing the role of a servant, he will learn. Do you understand? If you try to do it with what you have, you will miss everything. Do you understand? You must learn. You should learn. From the position of being a disciple of that leader, you should honestly learn and act as if you are replacing him. But you dislike that, don’t you? Do you dislike it or like it? You disliked it, right? "Yes." Don’t do that. Wherever you go, you are one family. A leader who has the responsibility to teach and save even one family member. You must not let even one family member die. If you let them die, if you cannot take responsibility, the family members will become a chain reaction of accountability.

How many people have you evangelized here? If there are many who have died and few who have been saved, then no matter how much you evangelize, it will not work. Such a leader must repent. He must wear a sackcloth and bow down and pretend to die. If that does not resolve the issue, all his sons and daughters will be indemnified. The law of indemnity is a fearful thing. I have shared these contents hoping that you will walk the right path as leaders. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Beloved Father, where else can there be a leader in this universe? We have come to know that there is none other than the perfect Father who created this universe. We have come to understand that you long for the appearance of the glorious sons and daughters who can embrace the True Parents as leaders, and that we must admire and yearn for such sons and daughters day and night. Now, we ask that you place us in the position of children who can be such.

Father, we know that the Unification Church has come this far because you have also gone through many valleys of tears, but this insignificant child has also shed tears secretly. You know that I have come this far with a heart worried about leaving conditions that could provoke sorrow before you. When I see the countless people who are infinitely striving to hold onto this insignificant being and to elevate this insignificant being to a position of praise, I cannot help but think that all of this is your glory and the merit of your labor.

Father, this Unification Church is not a church that is responsible for a side of flowing history, but a church that must block the flowing history and digest the whole. Therefore, we are a holy group that must have the highest heart in having a heart of love, the highest practice in practicing, and the highest sacrifice in sacrificing. We understand that being a holy group does not mean remaining a holy group simply because we have been chosen, but that we must remain in the position of wanting to sacrifice and sacrifice again.

There are no saints apart from those who sacrifice themselves while praying for blessings for all people. We understand that among those who can conclude the desires of the saints, there must be a connection of blood with the Father that must be planted on this earth by the sons and daughters who are to be the heirs of the Unification Church.

We have come to know that as those born with the lineage of Satan, we must reorganize that bloodline and inherit the bloodline of True Parents. We have now realized that we are those who have stood before you through that path and have received infinite blessings. We were unaware of the blessings we received and the position of blessed families, and we did not understand what kind of position the church leader who is responsible for choosing life holds. Now, we clearly understand that and ask that we do not become like the past.

Even if we die a hundred times and sacrifice a hundred times, we should not remember that; rather, we must seek a path of suffering that is greater than that, which is the position of the Father who has lost the entire universe, the position of Jesus and the Holy Spirit who must indemnify this, and the position of True Parents. When we think of this, we realize how foolish we have been to wish to avoid the path of tribulation and to escape the place of suffering until now.

Even though we are in a position to take responsibility for the suffering of the world beyond the nation, we, who have even tried to avoid the suffering of our own nation, now repent and awaken anew, and we strongly resolve to be a group that can stand in the position of your sons and daughters who can take on the path of death on behalf of the Father who is responsible for the suffering of not only our nation but the world.

In mid-August, in this beautiful season, we have gathered in Cheongpyeong to hold such a workshop, not to face the sadness that provokes despair and hopelessness, but to become the heirs of tomorrow's victory in hope and expectation. We, who have received a calling before the Father with naked bodies and red hearts, have gathered to resolve to start anew in the position of wanting to fulfill the commands you give us with our lives. We sincerely ask that this opportunity may allow us to regain the authority and dignity of sons that can please you and restore the authority of a leader, making this a period of light and value.

We must not forget the kind and orthodox thought of the Father, who does not abandon the historical connections that have come through suffering. We must endure to the end, so that we can enter into your realm of blessings and become sons and daughters who are not lacking in your love.

Today, I have spoken about what the path of a true leader is. To walk that path, one must possess the heart of True Parents and strategize to protect and find the children as True Parents. To do this, one must stand in the position of giving new things daily, which is the responsibility of a leader. We must clearly know that even if we are in a more difficult situation than others, we must stand in a position of greater sacrifice, caring for them and fulfilling the parental mission before them. I earnestly ask that you allow the church leaders gathered here this time to be such leaders. 

Let us once again realize how pitiful it is to have our own intentions and how many times we have made the Father feel sorrowful by saying what we want. Let us once again resolve to be individuals who are not lacking in establishing those who follow us as blessed sons and daughters. I earnestly ask that you allow us to clear ourselves and make a new start.

In this short time remaining, may you bless us so that we can become victorious princes and princesses who can remain in the restored garden you have allowed us, and may we be blessed to be leaders who can protect our lineage. If we cannot do so, please guide us even with a whip. 

I entrust everything to you, and I earnestly ask that you allow us to meet a victorious moment within your providential will. I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen. 

8) The Historical Completion Standards Viewed from Providence
Today, I would like to briefly speak on the topic of "Historical Completion Standards Viewed from Providence." When we think of "providence," we recall the restoration providence, or in other words, the salvation providence. Therefore, today's message also pertains to "Historical Completion Standards Viewed from Salvation Providence."

The Christian Sacrifice of Suffering
God has been carrying out the salvation providence for fallen humanity until now. In other words, God has been pushing the direction of providence to lead us, who have become the offspring of the enemy, to a certain historical standard of completion that He desires, namely the purpose standard of salvation providence.

In that process, families like Adam's, Noah's, Abraham's, Moses', Zechariah's, and Jesus' appeared, and a providential history centered on Christianity emerged to establish the Second Israel. However, to indemnify the providential history left behind from the First Israel, it must surpass the content that appeared in that providential history. If it is inferior to that, it cannot be indemnified. Just as it is impossible to erase written words without applying a greater force than that which was used to write them, the same applies here.

Therefore, Christianity has paid many sacrificial costs throughout history to establish the standards of victory that the First Israel could not achieve and failed to meet. Individuals were mobilized, families were mobilized, tribes were mobilized, nations were mobilized, and even the world was mobilized.

When viewed through the lens of the Roman Empire, it was a state with a stronger power than any other nation that could lead the world at that time. In that context, Christianity began in Israel, which was under the dominion of the Roman Empire, like a colony, and fought against Rome. Rome was a nation with global authority in terms of individuals, families, tribes, nations, and everything else.
