To do that, you must offer sacrifices for the nation. You must sacrifice your children and your wife. Do you understand? “Yes.” God has come out from such a position.

Didn’t God sacrifice His children and sacrifice Eve? Isn’t that an extremely miserable position for God, who is leading the history of restoration? Eve is God’s wife. The sons and daughters of Eve are God’s sons and daughters. Isn’t that right? “Yes.” It is the same. Therefore, you must be prepared to offer such sacrifices for the nation and run the path of suffering.

This time, I have cooperated little by little in building the church because you all stand in the position of having offered your families as sacrifices. What do we want to do by offering our families as sacrifices? We want to establish a tribal standard. That is precisely what the church is. Do you understand? “Yes.” It is not your house; it is the church. Those churches will become the point of contact with established churches in the future. That is why I have helped local churches this time. Otherwise, I would not help. They think the teacher will always help them. These little brats!

You must hold onto the nation and go through the process of sacrifice so that the nation can bow its head. This is our mission. Will you undertake such a mission or not? “We will.” Raise your hand if you are willing to undertake it.

If that happens, the history of the churches in this world will be woven through you, the Unification Church. Do you understand? “Yes.” It will be the history of the Unification Church, just like the history of the Old Testament and the New Testament. Now is the time of resurrection, so it is like the Old Testament era, right? The Old Testament, New Testament, and Completed Testament eras where we can establish a tradition. In other words, the time when the Unification Church merges with Christianity will be the Old Testament era, the time when it merges with the Republic of Korea will be the New Testament era, and the time when it merges with North Korea will be the Completed Testament era. If you look at it this way, there is no doubt.

So, will you pass through the process of sacrifice to establish the Old Testament era, or not? “We will.” If you pass through that process, will the Old Testament era be established or not? “It will be established.” If that happens, it will become the New Testament era, and when you enter the New Testament era, you will become the returning Lord of Jesus. Thus, when we complete the New Testament centered on the nation, we will have a unified nation, right? “Yes.” That is the same. It means that there will be no opposing nations. We are in such an era now. It is serious.
This is the global traditional history, which serves as the historical standard of completion. In other words, it is about centering on the history of your family and connecting your family to history. Do you understand? "Yes." A history is emerging in which your family can participate. If the teacher's family and your family become one, then your family will be liberated. After that, the family will unite and become the tribal Abel.

Furthermore, if you, as the tribal Abel, confront and subdue the tribal Cain with Christianity, you will become the national Abel. Is that right? "Yes." By becoming the national Abel and centering on the nation, it will only take a few people to subdue. That is how it is.

Therefore, with your right hand, you must hold onto the teacher, and with your left hand, you must hold onto the nation, embracing and defending it, and you must fight until 1972. Do you understand? "Yes." Let's run together with the teacher. If you cannot unite, who is more pitiful than you? Are there people in the world as pitiful as us? When we entered the Unification Church, did we come to meet our mother? Did we come to live happily among brothers?

We abandoned our parents, abandoned all our siblings, and abandoned all our relatives, and now we are being chased by the nation. What can't we do? Since we have abandoned our parents, we must live better than them, right? "Yes." We have abandoned our siblings and relatives, so we must unite, don't you think? If we cannot unite, we are the most pitiful in the world. Where can we complain in this world? Will we go back home and say, "Oh, mom and dad! I'm starving to death. I was foolish to leave, so I won't do that again"? Would we say that? If we were given a dog, we would have accepted it, but we cannot do that, can we? Even if we die, we cannot do that.

We must live united. Whether we live or die, we must be united. We must never be divided. We must not tremble. We are, after all, in a shared destiny. You and I are intertwined like a belt in a shared fate. We are in a position where we cannot cut off our ties. Therefore, if one dies here, two will die, and if two die, three will die, and if the number increases, the whole will die. This is the shared destiny we are in. Do you understand? "Yes." If we cannot unite here, there are no people as pitiful as us, but if we unite, are there people as happy as us? "No."

That is why, even if I call your name a thousand or ten thousand times, there is a name I want to call again, a name I want to call in my dreams, and that name is True Parents. Even if I call it a thousand or ten thousand times, there is a name I want to call again, and that name is the name of the sons and daughters of True Parents. Also, there is a family I want to call a thousand or ten thousand times and long for, which is the family of True Parents, and we wish to live together with the family of True Parents along with the nation. This is our wish. We want to serve together with the nation and sovereignty. This is not a statement centered on the teacher but a statement centered on Heaven's will. Do you understand? "Yes." Has it been achieved or not? "It has been achieved." 

It has, right? You must clearly understand this.

Everyone, the 1960s were a time of indemnity, a time of tears and pain. Those who have gone through such an era will become pitiful people who cannot raise their faces to Heaven if they cannot walk this path together as couples in this new providential history, which is the standard of completion in Heaven. If you are to embrace and love your children in such a position and shed tears, then you cannot be children of the Unification Church. You must bind your children from birth. You must not let them be sent to a place of death from birth, to a place of suffering.

So, regarding Hee-jin... The teacher knew such things. Would the parents not know? When Hee-jin died, I did not shed tears. I thought it was a hurdle I had to overcome. How do you think I felt seeing my child, who I sent to a place of death while I was determined to go the path of death for the sake of all people, collapse? I thought that my child had taken the path of death that I had to take. In this sense, if I am harsh, I am truly harsh.

Through this opportunity, I believe you have come to understand clearly what the current position centered on the foundation of providence is from a new perspective and new meaning. Do you understand? "Yes."

From a historical perspective, what position is our family in, how has our family's history unfolded, and what will this history become? History is just beginning now. Therefore, any mistakes made here will become mistakes for a thousand or ten thousand years. Just as the mistake of Adam and Eve for a day became a mistake for a thousand or ten thousand years, if we leave a mistake in this 21-year period, it will remain as a mistake for a thousand or ten thousand years. Do you understand? "Yes." The first, second, and third seven-year courses will now be forever gone. Do you think there will be such a course again? "No." There will never be again.

Let us make the 'historical standard of completion viewed from providence' come to fruition through us. In this age, the standard of individual completion will be born, and finally, the history of individual completion will rise up in history. The history that can represent all families, like a mold, will finally show its face, and the traditional standards of the expectation centered on families, like a mold, will appear as the purpose of providential history that God desires and humanity longs for. That time is now.

Centered on such families, the tribal model must emerge, and based on that model, a global tribal organization will be possible, and based on that, global restoration will be possible. Do you understand? "Yes."

Whether you go well or not will determine whether the period of global restoration is extended or shortened. The fate of global restoration is determined by you. Therefore, if we do not establish the history of tribal tradition here, the standard for educating the global tribes will not be determined. Is that right? "Yes."

To organize a global tribal realm and create a shining history and the origin of a brilliant culture, you must sweat from your backs and fingertips. Even if you sweat and shed tears, if that is not enough, we must resolve to cut open our bellies and bleed together before others die. We must be prepared to die together, even if it means killing our children and wives and stabbing ourselves, with the determination that we cannot die at the hands of our enemies. If we do not have a nation before us and do not have sovereignty, then the group that resolves to conclude there is the group of unification, the family of unification. You must clearly understand that this is our mainstream thought. Who will raise their hand to say they will do this? Oh, how holy! Will you really do it? "Yes." I have been deceived many times until now. Are you sure this time? "Yes." Let's see it happen.

Who will become the sacrifice to protect this nation and this people? You have come out dragging your twisted legs and limping steps to find that nation, so you are unfortunate men who cannot even die when the environment to find that nation is right in front of you. If I can find that nation by sacrificing my foot, I must step forward with the heart that I will offer it without regret. 

Even if I die, I must shine a brilliant history and open the well of tradition that can connect to a new resurrection in the valley of death of historical eras. This is the position of those of us who are responsible for providence.

Such times do not always exist. They are short. The 21 years pass like a dream. "When did ten years pass? Was there such a history?" It passes in the blink of an eye. That is why, even though the teacher is over 50 years old... Before coming here today, I spoke for nearly six hours, and when I tried to finish and come down, my legs stiffened and I stumbled, right? So, I leaned on the desk to get down. Even so, I thought, "Let's go to Cheongpyeong. These kids are waiting, so I have to go." That is why I came here. I will endure like this until my 80s.

My wish is to fulfill what I resolved before God, to achieve my desires, to worship God, and to meet the day when I can pull out the sword I had stuck and ask Him to strike the enemy, and then to close my eyes and die. This is the wish of the man you call your teacher. You must know that there was a journey of struggle in which I fought with a heart full of purpose, unable to do anything while seeing my children lying in misery, unable to sleep from hunger. You are not the only ones who have come out like this. The traditional thought of patriots arises in such positions. Therefore, you must beautifully, gracefully, and obediently carry on that tradition.

Only then will the 'historical standard of completion viewed from providence' be born through us. Do you understand? "Yes." Here, the standard of our age, this era, is determined. To draw gold with this standard, we must draw each line accurately so that anyone can say it is unmistakable.

The teacher has repeatedly said, "Establish the tradition." You have heard this many times. You must establish the tradition correctly. If you cannot establish the tradition, you will perish. Tradition is about connecting and establishing the patriotic thought of that nation. Therefore, there is no time other than this era to establish the ideological tradition. Do you understand?

The historical standard of completion remains from the age of the covenant. The fact that you have welcomed this era with your wife is a surprising and astonishing thing. It is more difficult than the unification of the world. The unification of the world starts from here. Therefore, you can be happier than anyone in any era. Since it is such a position, there are both sorrow and joy intertwined. You must understand that you must have the subjectivity to digest all such sorrows and joys, which is the mission of you, the Unification Church members, especially those responsible for local churches.

During your time as church leaders, you must show the traditional path of Heaven's Kingdom to all people and lay down a certain path, like a highway. If you do so, you will survive for a thousand or ten thousand years in their blood, flesh, and spirit. Do you understand? "Yes." Even if there are joyful events, you will look at the tombstone of your grave, and if there are mountains you used to cross, you will recite history while crossing those mountains, saying, "May you receive this joy." You will become such ancestors. That is a meaningful life. Do you understand? "Yes."

What blessing is there in living a life of eating, laughing, and dancing on the main road and then going to the grave? In the grave of such a person, only grass will grow, but in the grave of a person who shed blood for the nation, flowers will bloom as long as that nation is alive.

When the teacher dies, will you come to visit the teacher's grave? "Yes." In what form will you come? It will be a worry even if you come. When you come to the teacher's grave and say, "Teacher, I have come. So-and-so has come," the spirit of the deceased should welcome you, saying, "Ah, you who I hoped would come, have you come?" You must become such people... Is that not so? "Yes." The problem is significant. So what must you do? You must become beautiful seeds, bear beautiful fruits, and expand the foundation of glory, hoping to come as precious and praised people, right? Is that not so? "Yes."

Also, it is the same when you come to visit while the teacher is still alive. Will you come to visit or not? "I will go." How will you come? Will you come to the teacher and say, "Oh, teacher, I am about to die. Please help me"? The teacher cannot do such things even in death. The teacher cannot pray, "Father! I have become a beggar, so please help me. This is a big problem. Please help me," just because I lost all the money I had in a week. If I have taken responsibility, I must devote all my sincerity and bear that pain alone. That is how it must be. Will you do the same?

You will not act like a beggar after sleeping well and becoming cowardly. You will work without sleeping. Even if you cannot work when you are young, you will work without sleeping even when you are old. You must go the valuable path knowing this and that.

Then, when will the historical standard of completion of the new nation remain? It is not the Old Testament era, nor the New Testament era, but the era of the covenant. The history of the new nation will remain from this era of the covenant. It will sprout from here. The original source of teachings will also arise from here, the main thread of thought will also arise from here, the laws of justice to judge the satanic world will also arise from here, and the methods to eliminate evil will also arise from here. So, were you born well or poorly? "I was born well."

You were born well, but if you cannot take responsibility here, you will become the most unfortunate person. In that case, it will not only be your downfall but you will become a pitiful monster that brings down the whole. Even so, were you born well? Were you born well or poorly? "I was born well." To be able to say you were born well, you must live and overcome the brink of death many times. You must become a person who can step over the path of death to go before God without hesitation, even after seeing your children facing death. Can you do that? "Yes." If you cannot, you will be worse than Jesus and less than Abraham. The one who bears the final responsibility for completion must be able to be more loyal than anyone who has been loyal in history. 

Is that right? "Yes."

Now is a wonderful era in providence. In the past, sacrifices were made to God with paper or objects, or Jesus himself, the Son of God, became a sacrifice, but now you must be willing to sacrifice your sons and daughters, your wives, and even yourselves. The time is such. Do you understand? Therefore, are you worse than Jesus or better? "Better." When God faces you, are you better than you were in Jesus' time? "I will be better." 

In this era, such seemingly absurd words can be established. Did Jesus ever send his wife to evangelize? Did he send his sons and daughters to say, "Let's go evangelize with mom and dad"? "He did not." So, you are better than Jesus, right? You are better, right? "Yes."

Thus, you are in a wonderful era. Do you understand, or not? Do you roughly understand? "Yes." The historical standard of completion viewed from providence cannot be established at any time. What will happen if the teacher dies? Will it pass by or remain? "It will pass." The time will pass. If the teacher dies without fulfilling this will, what will you do? "It will remain." 

If it remains, what will you do? "I will do that instead..." 

That is why the teacher teaches you in such a way that it penetrates your very bones. Therefore, you must clearly understand what the teacher is doing and at what stage it is now.
If you can clearly understand what exists, then in the next stage, you will be able to think about what to do and how to do it, and even if the teacher dies, you will be able to inherit the intention and set the completion standard. That is why the teacher is teaching you these things now. Do you understand what time it is now? "Yes." In the past, established church members devoted themselves to the atonement of the time of Cain. They worked hard to become like Cain. They worked diligently to atone for the shameful position of Cain. Do you understand? "Yes." Then, why do you work hard? "To become Abel...." To become a shameful Abel, to become a victorious Abel? Abel is Abel, but it is to become an Abel better than Jesus.

We are now putting our heart into standing in the position of Abel, who bears the responsibility for the restoration of the nation. Do you understand? "Yes." Even if we put in the same effort, we are on a higher dimension. That is why, even if we walk the same path with the same effort and in the same position, when we go to the spirit world, they must be under our dominion. Do you understand? "Yes." So, should we put in more effort than the established church pastors or less? "We should put in more effort." This is something that is obvious without needing to ask.

Now, do you roughly understand? "Yes." Now you will think, "Ah, we need to do this until 1972. That is why the teacher said the time of registration is coming!" Do you understand? "Yes." If you do not allow men with wives to participate in the time of registration, it may not be that they die standing, but they may die crawling on the ground. Why? Because they cannot stand the pressure from their own children. Such a time is coming. They will become miserable parents who hear from their children, "Oh, what did you do, mother and father?" I think like that. They will make their children’s eyes flash with anger, saying, "Why did you come first and make it like this?" Such a time is coming. If that time does not come, I may have to make it come. This is not a joke. Do you understand? "Yes."

That is why the teacher teaches our children, "Our father is the best father in the world, and our mother is the best mother in the world. Your parents are the only mother and father in the world." This thought must be instilled. Do you understand? You must also inherit this thought and make your children think like that day and night.

To do that, you must first become the filial sons and daughters that have never existed in world history. You must leave behind such thoughts. You must become a couple that can say, "Our family has values that do not exist in this world." This is inheriting such thoughts. Do you understand? "Yes."

You must leave behind the thought that "Our relatives do not like to live together even for a thousand years, but prefer to gather more." That is why the teacher wants the nations and peoples of the world to live together under one fence. You must understand that this is the mainstream unification thought. Do you understand?

Keep your eyes wide open and run vigorously towards your destination. You must remember the words the teacher spoke today, on the evening of August 17, 1971. And you must return with the heart to illuminate history forever. Do you understand? "Yes." You must change after hearing this message. Will you change or not? "We will change."

Now, you must look straight ahead. The teacher's purpose and your purpose are the same. Is that right? "Yes." Therefore, even if you suffer, you must suffer together, cry together, and rejoice together. However, since there is an order in work, to save the greater good, you must sacrifice the smaller family. Can you take care of your children and wife when you say you will sacrifice the family? You must clearly understand this.

Now is the time to set the historical completion standard. It is the time to set the individual completion standard, the family completion standard, the tribal completion standard, the national completion standard, and the state completion standard. Therefore, only with the traditions established at this time can the world be melted. This means creating the yeast of the world. It will become a strong sword that can cut off any nation's tradition.

So, everyone, if the teacher says to cross the 38th parallel, will everyone be mobilized or not? "They will be mobilized." Right now, these Korean soldiers, the squad leaders and battalion leaders, are all thinking of packing their bags and running away. The teacher thinks it would be better to train thousands of squad leaders and thousands of company leaders. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Knowing this, you must go out to establish the historical completion standard. The historical completion standard is what God desires, what history desires, what humanity desires, and what the teacher desires. That iron mold will be created. Even if the materials or qualities are different, the shapes must be the same. Do you understand? The shapes must be the same. Our families' shapes are like that, right?

Now, the lives of our Unification Church members are miserable, right? The living conditions are miserable. However, if it can make God happy to sacrifice their children, there are people who would willingly offer their children to the path of death. That is not a bad thing. Such things will all become traditions. The more miserable the story, the more it will shine for thousands and tens of thousands of years.

The teacher has said this before: "A family that has martyrs in the historical age centered on unification thought is blessed." In the teacher's family, Hee-jin went as a representative in 1969. At that time, the teacher commanded that everyone must be mobilized this year. Since 1969 was the second year of the three-year course, everyone had to be mobilized. At that time, Hee-jin said, "Since not everyone is going out, shouldn't I go alone?" And then he said he was going to Gimcheon. At that time, the teacher thought there was a Gimcheon in Gyeonggi Province and thought he was going there. If he had known he was going to Gimcheon in Gyeongsang Province, he would not have sent him. He knew it was a time to be careful and hold each other while being within the fence. But he forgot. That’s how he went. Thus, Hee-jin became the first martyr of our family. By shedding the blood of martyrdom as a flower bud that has not yet bloomed, he can participate in the glorious position, and the shining value of that will remain as a tradition in the historical age, so the teacher thinks it is a proud path he took.

Then, should your family have such sons and daughters or not? "They should." The teacher and you are the same in this regard. Therefore, knowing the value of this era and the fateful connection of this time, may God come to this point where He connects the traditional achievements of the ancestors and may it be a shining fruit. I hope you remember this well. Do you understand? "Yes."

<Prayer> Beloved Father, please remember your young sons gathered here. Let your holy hand of grace come upon this place where we realize our foolish past and awaken to the serious history behind it. Father, if this period is a time of gratitude, we must realize it is also a time of fear. Those who were foolish and did not understand the Father’s circumstances now feel they have become mature sons who can understand and empathize with the Father’s painful circumstances. They must not turn back from the fateful path they must take toward the Father. 

Since we have entrusted it to you, whether it is miserable or glorious, it is yours. When we think about the weight of value, we come to know that misery is precious, not glory. If there are sons and daughters who would become offerings that can be split in one blow, you will be able to welcome the time to shake off the grievances of thousands and tens of thousands of years because of them, and also, when we think that your heart of compassion and sympathy can erase the foundation of grievances for all people, let us realize how precious and holy the place we are in today is. 

If we do not fulfill the duty of filial piety and loyalty, even if we live, we will be dead souls, and if we cannot do that, we must know that the path of a man is to collapse while calling out the Father’s name. May this period be a time to renew our resolve, Father, I earnestly wish and hope for this. 

Father, I know that there are circumstances that cannot be spoken to anyone in the world centered around the family. However, I know that your sad circumstances are swirling around here. Centered on the heart of restoration, we can feel the sorrow that Jesus endured from the position of a living parent, standing in the same position as the Father. Even though the outward appearance is miserable, we must understand that this is a victorious place where we can inherit your heart hidden in history. We must know that your heart is seeping into the place where we look at our pale children, where the heart reaches its peak and feels like it will burst. 

We can discover how the Father feels when looking at young children eating barley rice with chopsticks, and although those children may be pale, they are not children going to die; they are children who can go to a hopeful place as heirs of the kingdom of heaven, so we must think that they are not pitiful but proud children who can receive heavenly blessings and sympathy. As unworthy children before the Father, having the moment to embrace the Father’s neck and weep while looking at such children is something that cannot be exchanged for thousands and tens of thousands of years. May they realize this.

If there are those who love such children, let them have the heart of a parent who thinks of the reality of affection and is willing to repay and be grateful with their lives. If someone gives a piece of bread for such children, let them think of that person as a benefactor who has received the grace of a thousand years of history and resolve to return blessings to them. 

This time, we can feel and know that we have formed connections with those who can bless those who give a piece of bread or a bowl of water to our beloved sons and daughters in this sad historical journey. Let us engrave this deeply in our hearts and bones. 

Every time we stand in such a place, let us think of Jesus’ situation, hold onto the Father, and shed tears. Let us know that there is a holy moment in our family where the grievances of Jesus, who could not receive parental love and disappeared, can be resolved, and we can say that such conditions of pride exist in our family. May there be times to inherit such blessed places. 

We thought there was a tribe that would welcome us, but seeing that there is no such tribe, how much have we longed for such a tribe? We hope that we can have the heart of the Father, who wants to sacrifice everything for such a tribe and love it deeply, and even if we become servants before that tribe, we can have a heart of gratitude. Let them believe that there is a reality that if the Zechariah family had to be like that, it must be restored in the form of a family that has compensated for that. 

We know that a fortunate era is before us, where sovereignty can fluctuate at our fingertips, transcending nations and peoples. When we think that this fortunate era is not something I alone will meet, but that it is allowed to be welcomed together with parents, wives, and children, we must be able to shed tears and be grateful as a whole. 

Father, please embrace and love the Unification Church that you wanted to love, and if there are your sons and daughters whom you wanted to chastise, do not hesitate to whip them. So that as a nation without abundance, no one who started falls behind, and even if we wander in the wilderness for 40 years after crossing the Red Sea, may we be remembered before the Father as a group that can walk together with the heart to die on the path of heaven. 

At this time, in the name of the Father and as a husband, I swear on behalf of my wife, my children, my descendants, and on behalf of the entire family, tribe, nation, and state, may you receive this and may there be no more acts of rebellion against the Father. I earnestly ask that this time be remembered as a time you can remember. 

On that dear and longed-for day when the historical completion standard is established, looking at that boundary line that we have sought and sought again, may we become a holy multitude that will not lose that glorious moment, even if we die a million times, and may this become the tradition of history and the shining pride of the tribe. 

I earnestly hope that our Unification Church will become the foundation of victory, and at this time, I have conveyed your words to the young sons and daughters, so may they become a group that knows how to be grateful for the grace of the unfulfilled longing that melts their bones and flesh. May they also become a holy multitude that fulfills the priestly duty of guarding the heavenly sanctuary and receives blessings from the Father without lacking anything. 

Please remember the remaining time tomorrow. May the weaving of your will, intertwined in busy days, be connected through Asia to the world, allowing us to receive heavenly fortune, and may your victorious path be strongly and proudly connected to our movements and directions of body and mind centered on the Korean territory. I ask once again, and I pray all these things in the name of the True Parents. Amen. *
